Optional `debounceMs` override (tests use 0). Returns `CanvasPreviewDataMap` keyed by saved_view_id with `{status: loading|success|error, data?, previous?, error?}` discriminated union; previous-on-loading carries last-known-good data for optimistic-stale rendering (Lock 5a). Error classification via `classifyError`: 404→`view_not_found`, 403→`permission_denied`, ERR_NETWORK / no response / 5xx→`network_error` with `network_class: true`, else generic `fetch_failed`. Cleanup on unmount aborts all in-flight controllers. - **2026-05-21 — Sub-arc WB-4a shipped (uncommitted) — Widget Builder shell + canvas + auto-save + Publish + r106 migration.** First operator-facing Widget Builder sub-arc per investigation `7b9e19a` + WB-4a/WB-4b split recommendation. (2) WidgetDefinition model + Pydantic serializer carry the new column with full doc comments anchoring Area 2 lock. (3) Three new API endpoints at `/api/v1/widget-definitions/*`: `POST /` creates a new composed widget with a default empty flex-stack root (tier_scope='vertical' default; composition_version=1; published_composition_blob=NULL); `PUT /{slug}/draft` permissive auto-save (accepts any dict shape; full validation deferred to Publish per Area 5); `POST /{slug}/publish` full Pydantic + custom validator pass, copies composition_blob → published_composition_blob, increments composition_version, returns HTTP 422 with structured `{code: "composition_invalid", errors: [...]}` on invalid; `GET /{slug}` for editor load. Slug collision auto-disambiguates to `{base}-N`. (5) Frontend canonical `WidgetDefinition` interface extended with `published_composition_blob?: unknown | null` (purely additive optional; ZERO existing consumer updates needed per the WB-3 audit pattern). (6) `dispatchWidgetDefinition` now reads **published_composition_blob FIRST**; falls back to composition_blob ONLY when published is NULL AND draft is non-NULL (legacy r105-backfill case OR authoring canvas draft-preview path explicitly passing draft); falls through to hand-coded widget path when both blobs null. Existing hand-coded render path UNCHANGED. (7) Studio route `/studio/widget-builder/{slug?}` mounted in `StudioShell.tsx` analogous to `builder/focuses` precedent; slug-optional (no slug → landing card with "+ New Widget"; explicit slug → editor); `RESERVED_FIRST_SEGMENTS` extended with `widget-builder` + `builder` to forward-defend future vertical-slug authoring against collision. (8) `WidgetBuilderPage` shell at `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/components/widget-builder/WidgetBuilderPage.tsx` (~470 LOC) — three-pane layout (AtomPalette left / WidgetCanvas center / inspector stub right); top chrome with editable widget name + tier indicator badge (`platform` / `vertical` per record) + draft-state indicator ("Saved" / "Saving…" / "Draft (unpublished)" / "Save failed") + Publish button + canvas root flex config selects (direction column/row + gap sm/md/lg); on slug change loads via `widgetBuilderService.get(slug)`; landing flow dispatches `widgetBuilderService.create()` then navigates to new slug. (9) `AtomPalette` (`AtomPalette.tsx`, ~150 LOC) — 2 sections per Area 3 lock (Content & Visual: text_label / value_display / icon / status_badge / divider / image; Container & Interactive: conditional_container / repeater_atom / button); each tile is a `useDraggable` source carrying `{source: "palette", atom_type}` in dnd-kit data; Lucide icons per the suggested mapping (Type / Hash / Star / Tag / Minus / Image / MousePointer / Box / List); minimal visual chrome per Area 3 restraint principle. (10) `WidgetCanvas` (`WidgetCanvas.tsx`, ~260 LOC) build-new flex-stack substrate (NOT FF-2 reuse per Area 1 lock — does NOT import PlacedWidgetCore / WidgetFreeFormLayer / FreeFormPlacedWidget); canvas root renders ComposedWidget for WYSIWYG preview (canvas IS the preview); overlay layer with `InsertionIndicator` between-sibling drop zones + `ContainerDropTarget` drop-as-child targets on container atoms; empty-canvas "Drag atoms here" affordance; click-to-select with selection ring outline; root flex direction + gap_token honored from the canvas-root container's config. (12) Atom-tree manipulation pure helpers (`atom-tree-helpers.ts`, ~200 LOC) — `makeDefaultAtomNode` produces Pydantic-compliant defaults per atom_type (button → action_kind='navigate'; conditional_container → direction='column' + gap_token='sm'; repeater_atom → empty binding_id + children + direction='column' + spacing='normal'; etc.); `insertAtomAt` / `moveAtomTo` / `removeAtom` / `findParentId` / `setRootDirection` / `setRootGap`; repeater_atom mirror discipline preserved (config.children kept in sync with AtomNode.children). (13) `widgetBuilderService` (`services/widget-builder-service.ts`, ~145 LOC) — thin axios wrapper; `WidgetBuilderApiError` carries status + structured detail; URL-encoded slug in path. - **2026-05-21 — Sub-arc WB-2 shipped (uncommitted) — ComposedWidget runtime renderer.** Second widget-builder sub-arc per investigation `5771fc0`. Establishes the runtime interpretation layer (hybrid Model C per Area 5) that renders WB-1 composition_blob into the same DOM substrate hand-coded widgets render into. **FRONTEND-ONLY.** No backend changes, no Alembic migrations; migration head unchanged at `r105_widget_definitions_composition_extension`. Pre-flight: HEAD verified `7eb1280` (WB-1 Foundation). **What WB-2 ships:** (1) `ComposedWidget` React component (`frontend/src/lib/widget-builder/runtime/ComposedWidget.tsx`) — single component (NOT codegen) that parses CompositionBlob via WB-1's `parseCompositionBlob` codec + recursively dispatches; emits `<div data-composed-widget-root="true" data-widget-id="...">` as the hit-testable inner-div per Area 6 dual-wrapping lock + hover-fix d9ffd90 finding. (2) `AtomRenderer` (`./AtomRenderer.tsx`) — recursive atom-type dispatcher with variant filtering (visible_in_variants check against optional `variantId` prop) + binding resolution + exhaustive switch over 8 atom_types; ConditionalContainerRenderer wrapped via `registerComponent` (the only Phase 1 atom with children gets its own `data-component-name="wb-conditional-container-atom"` boundary), other 7 leaf atoms render inside ComposedWidget's hit-test inner-div. (3) 8 placeholder atom renderers (`./atoms/index.tsx`) — semantic-HTML-only Phase 1 UI (text_label `<span>`, value_display `<span>`, icon `<span>[icon:name]`, status_badge `<span>[badge]`, divider `<hr>`, button `<button type="button">` with no-op onClick, image `<span>[image]`, conditional_container `<div>{children}</div>`); all emit `data-atom-type` + `data-atom-id` for editor + integration test introspection. WB-3 swaps placeholder UI for real typography/theme/icon UI without breaking the dispatch contract. (4) `resolveBinding` helper (`./resolveBinding.ts`) — Phase 1 placeholder: literal → `literal_value`; field_path → `[bound:${field_path}]` placeholder string. WB-6 makes this real saved-view resolution; consumer interface stable. (5) "composed" widget renderer registration (`./register.tsx`) — side-effect import wired in `App.tsx` at app bootstrap, mirroring the established `widgets/foundation/register.ts` pattern (SavedViewWidget noted as the canonical config-driven precedent). Adapter bridges `WidgetRendererProps` to `ComposedWidget`, extracting `composition_blob` from `config.composition_blob` per dispatch convention. (6) `dispatchWidgetDefinition` helper (`./dispatch.ts`) — single additive entry-point that branches: composition_blob populated → "composed" renderer + stashes blob into config.composition_blob; composition_blob null → existing `getWidgetRenderer(widget_id)` path UNCHANGED. The helper does NOT mutate caller's config object (test-asserted). Existing callers of `getWidgetRenderer` (Canvas, BottomSheet, StackRail, StackExpandedOverlay, PulsePiece, PinnedSection) continue to work unchanged — hand-coded widget render path explicitly UNCHANGED. **Tests shipped:** 6 new test files / 61 new test cases — `resolveBinding.test.ts` (7), `atoms/atoms.test.tsx` (18), `AtomRenderer.test.tsx` (16), `ComposedWidget.test.tsx` (7), `dispatch.test.tsx` (5 — including ComposedWidget-inside-PlacedWidgetCore-shaped-DOM integration assertion verifying FF substrate composition correctness + hand-coded regression preservation), `source-shape.test.ts` (6 source-shape gates per DECISIONS.md entry 31 pattern — catches future reverts of load-bearing structural elements: `data-composed-widget-root`, `parseCompositionBlob(` invocation, registerComponent wrap on conditional_container, exhaustive 8-case switch, 8 atom-renderer exports, both dispatch branches). **Architectural notes:** (a) ComposedWidget receives a flexible `ComposedWidgetInput` shape (widget_id + composition_blob) rather than the full `components/widgets/types.ts::WidgetDefinition` interface — the existing TS interface doesn't yet declare composition_blob, and the loose-typed boundary lets WB-3+ catalog work proceed without breaking WB-2. (b) The "composed" registration adapter pulls composition_blob from `config.composition_blob` because `WidgetRendererProps` doesn't have a widget-definition-level axis — `dispatchWidgetDefinition` stashes it there at dispatch time. This keeps existing canvas registry shape untouched. (c) Defensive throws on null composition_blob (dispatch contract violation), missing root_atom_id, and unknown atom_type (TS exhaustive guard). Dangling child / binding_id refs render placeholder (`[unbound:id]`) rather than crash — production load must remain resilient even when backend semantic validator drifts. (d) 2-level nesting cap (Q-5) trusted from WB-1 validator at write time; runtime renderer doesn't re-enforce. (e) `register.ts` (the canonical visual-editor HOC at line 215) NOT modified; only one-line side-effect addition to `App.tsx`. No modifications to `widget-renderers.ts` / `PlacedWidgetCore.tsx` / any FF / F-series substrate (regression preservation). **Gates:** tsc clean; vitest 238 files / 3236 tests passing (one test todo, no regressions vs WB-1 baseline; two transient parallel-mode flakes observed across multiple runs in unrelated test files, confirmed pre-existing via final clean run); build clean (5.75s); bundle delta absolute +8.87 kB (6,124.30 → 6,133.17 kB) / +0.145%; gzipped +2.65 kB (1,473.24 → 1,475.89) / +0.180%. - **2026-05-21 — Resize live preview fix arc shipped (uncommitted) — Option A commit-on-tick; first FF-series Playwright spec exercising pointer-driven gesture; FF-6 inspector live W/H updates as Option A side effect.** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `57d7667` per process canon (resize-live-preview investigation). Single combined dispatch against locks in `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-resize-live-preview.md`. **Production fix**: added `parseResizeHandleId` branch to `handleDragMove` in `FocusBuilderPage.tsx` parallel-shape to the existing `handleDragEnd` resize branch (lines 822-880); branch RETURNS before the snap-line early-exit (resize does not participate in snap-to-alignment per investigation §5). **Architectural refinement during build — drag-start placement snapshot**: investigation locked "parallel-shape to handleDragEnd resize branch" but Option A as literally specified would compound the resize across ticks because @dnd-kit's `e.delta` is CUMULATIVE-from-drag-start while the resize branch reads `currentPlacement` from state — after the first tick, state has already moved; tick 2 would add cumulative delta (50px) to the already-moved width (265px) → 315px instead of correct 290px. Surfaced by JSDOM mid-drag test failing with final width 365 (5 ticks compounded) vs expected 290. **Fix**: new `resizeInitialPlacementRef: useRef<{ placementId, x, y, width, height } | null>` captured at `handleDragStart` when the active drag id matches a resize-handle shape; BOTH the new `handleDragMove` resize branch AND the existing `handleDragEnd` resize branch read `currentPlacement` from this snapshot instead of from placement state; ref cleared on dragEnd + dragCancel. Idempotency preserved: handleDragEnd's redundant final commit fires the same cumulative delta against the same snapshot → same `computeResizeCommit` output → no-op merge in the FF-7 functional setter. This refinement was NOT pre-locked in the investigation; surfaced during JSDOM verification and resolved within the fix arc per the investigation's §8 architectural-surprise canon ("handleDragEnd + Option-A handleDragMove would have identical bodies" was true at the time of writing the investigation but false after the first tick mutates state — a load-bearing detail the investigation missed). **Aspect-ratio Shift detection: NOT implemented.** The existing handleDragEnd resize branch does NOT preserve aspect ratio via Shift; `computeResizeCommit` has no such parameter; the FocusBuilderPage.tsx:505-506 canonical comment explicitly notes "@dnd-kit's DragMoveEvent does NOT expose the activator's current modifier state mid-gesture." Implementing aspect-ratio preservation would require (a) extending `computeResizeCommit` (DO NOT MODIFY per scope discipline), (b) tracking shiftKeyHeldRef document-level listener parallel to altKeyHeldRef. Out of scope for this arc; flagged for future operator-validation arc if needed. **Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied (BOTH paths)**: (a) **JSDOM** — stashed `FocusBuilderPage.tsx` production change, ran new mid-drag test → FAILED at `expect(midWidth1).toBeGreaterThan(initialWidth)` with `expected 240 to be greater than 240` (pre-fix handleDragMove ignores resize handles; width unchanged across ticks); restored → PASSED with midWidth1=265, midWidth2=290, finalWidth=290. (b) **Playwright + source-shape gate** — stashed production change, ran source-shape regression gate (which reads FocusBuilderPage.tsx as a string via Node fs + asserts `parseResizeHandleId`/`computeResizeCommit`/`updateWidget` regex matches inside handleDragMove body) → FAILED at `expect(body).toMatch(/parseResizeHandleId/)`; restored → PASSED. The Playwright inline-fixture spec exercises generic chromium pointer events but does NOT exercise production handleDragMove (inline fixture has its own JS pointer-event wiring); the source-shape gate is the LOAD-BEARING pre-fix-fails / post-fix-passes assertion per the hover-fix arc d9ffd90 precedent. Inline fixture reproduces the operator-observable SHAPE (positioned widget whose dimensions update during pointer-drag on a child handle); production-path regression guard is the source-shape gate. Spec lives at `frontend/tests/e2e/focus-builder-freeform-resize-preview.spec.ts` (~190 LOC). **Test surface**: 1 new mid-drag JSDOM test at `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` ("FF-4 — resize via e handle previews live per drag-move tick (mid-drag width grows)" ~115 LOC); 1 new source-shape regression gate at `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` ("FF-4 source-shape gate — handleDragMove contains a parseResizeHandleId branch" ~25 LOC); 1 new Playwright spec at `frontend/tests/e2e/focus-builder-freeform-resize-preview.spec.ts` (~190 LOC inline-fixture + 1 test "widget dimensions update during drag (not only at release)" with 4 assertions: preBBox baseline, midDragBBox1 > preBBox, midDragBBox2 > midDragBBox1, finalBBox ≈ midDragBBox2 within 2px). - **2026-05-20 (later) — Read-only investigation arc produced: `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-resize-live-preview.md` filed (uncommitted); locks live-resize-preview fix shape; fix arc pending dispatch.** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `d9ffd90` per process canon (hover-state staging-regression fix). Zero production / test code touched. Investigation triggered by operator staging verification of `d9ffd90`: hover-state working; UUID leak fix holding; relatedTarget edge case working. New finding surfaced — **resize doesn't preview during drag** (widget stays at original dimensions throughout drag; only updates to final dimensions at pointer-release). FF-3 drag-to-move DOES preview live; FF-4 drag-resize does NOT. **Architectural root cause locked**: `@dnd-kit/core`'s `useDraggable` returns a `transform: {x, y}` object that updates per pointer-move tick. FF-3 at `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx:199-201` consumes this transform as `style.transform: translate3d(...)` on the widget wrapper — the OS compositor GPU-translates the widget under the cursor; no state mutation; no rowsDraft churn; preview is FREE. FF-4 resize handles at `ResizeHandleOverlay.tsx:150-157` call useDraggable but DO NOT destructure `transform` (and couldn't usefully consume it anyway — translating an 8×8 handle doesn't resize the parent widget). The widget's dimensions at `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx:247-248` are state-controlled via `placement.width` / `placement.height`; the ONLY way to change them visually is to commit a state mutation. The page-level `handleDragMove` at `FocusBuilderPage.tsx:1114-1182` early-exits for resize-handle drag ids (line 1117-1118 — `parseFreeFormDraggableId` returns null for `<placement-uuid>-handle-<position>` shape; no resize branch exists). At drag-end, `handleDragEnd:836-880` commits via `computeResizeCommit` + `updateWidget`. Net: handles drag (their own translate3d), widget dimensions never mutate during drag, no preview. **Fundamental asymmetry**: @dnd-kit's transform model handles POSITION cheaply via CSS translate; DIMENSIONS require state-mediated rendering through `placement.width`/`.height` → React re-render. **Four fix options enumerated + audited**: (A) commit-on-tick — add `parseResizeHandleId` branch in handleDragMove; dispatch `updateWidget` per tick; lowest implementation cost (~30 LOC production); composes cleanly with FF-7 functional setter race-fix (was designed for rapid successive calls); 60Hz re-render of all canvas widgets but with stable React keys + bounded canvas size (≤20 widgets) within frame budget; Q-26 debounced save absorbs network cost via coalescing; FF-6 inspector inputs update LIVE during drag (W/H counter up in real time). (B) canvas-level ghost state — page tracks `resizeGhost`; rendering reads ghost or placement; cleaner re-render scope but requires prop drilling through canvas → layer → widget; FF-6 inputs would NOT update during drag (breaks bidirectional sync). (C) CSS inline width/height delta during drag — useDndMonitor inside FreeFormPlacedWidget; cheapest re-render footprint; requires duplicating per-handle math at render path; FF-6 inputs do not update. (D) per-widget local ghost — each widget owns its own monitor subscription; clean separation; N subscriptions for N widgets (negligible at typical scale); FF-6 inputs do not update. **Locked recommendation: Option A**. Reasoning: (1) symmetry with FF-6 W/H inputs — when operator types W=400 in inspector, widget updates instantly via FF-1 bidirectional sync; resize gesture is the cursor-driven equivalent; Option A preserves this mental model. (2) lowest implementation surface — ~30 LOC new branch parallel to existing handleDragEnd resize branch. (3) composes cleanly with FF-7 functional setter discipline (race-fix designed for this workload). (4) Q-26 debounced save absorbs network cost. (5) re-render concern theoretical not measured; React.memo on placement props is surgical mitigation if needed. (6) doesn't entangle snap-during-resize question (deferred per §5). **Architectural inconsistency Option A introduces**: FF-6 inputs WOULD update live during resize, but FF-6 inputs do NOT update live during drag-to-move (because FF-3 uses CSS translate not state). One gesture updates inputs live; the other doesn't. Flagged for operator hand-validation post-fix; not blocking. **Snap-to-alignment during resize: DEFERRED** to follow-up investigation. Q-11 locked snap for drag-to-move; `computeSnapAdjustment` takes a `dragPosition` for BBox-vs-edges math; resize-snap requires per-edge math (which edge is moving snaps to a neighbor's edge), meaningfully different. Operator signal hasn't surfaced "resize should snap" yet. Adding now expands fix arc from ~165 LOC to ~400+ LOC for unvalidated need. **Test substrate strategy**: JSDOM coverage via @dnd-kit's KeyboardSensor (Tab to focus handle, Space to grab, Arrow keys to delta-emit, Space to commit; assert rowsDraft mutates per-tick) — Q-40 canon applies. JSDOM pointer-event coverage remains unreliable (known gap per Q-40 generalization extended by hover-fix arc). Playwright spec required: hover widget → grab SE handle → mouse.down + mouse.move to intermediate position + assert bbox during gesture + mouse.up + assert final bbox. Source-shape regression gate per hover-fix precedent: unit test reads FocusBuilderPage.tsx source-string + asserts `parseResizeHandleId` appears inside handleDragMove body; catches accidental removal during future refactors. **Implementation surface estimate**: ~35 production LOC + ~50 JSDOM test LOC + ~80 Playwright LOC = ~165 LOC. **Fix arc dispatch shape: single combined arc** — production branch + JSDOM keyboard test + source-shape gate + Playwright spec; one commit; one staging verification cycle. Operator hand-validation: drag each of 8 handle positions; widget should glide dimension-wise throughout drag; release dimensions match. **Architectural surprises**: (1) `useDraggable` returns `transform` that's wholly unused for resize handles — handles still receive attributes/listeners/setNodeRef for the drag-end commit path; the visual transform is dropped (correctly — handles are edge-anchored, shouldn't translate). Surfaces the asymmetry: @dnd-kit transform model is position-only by design. (2) `handleDragMove` predates resize handles or was authored only for drag-to-move; the early-exit at line 1118 is correct for snap-lines (only drag-to-move computes snap) but accidentally also short-circuits live-resize. Classic case of one handler doing two jobs, correct for one. (3) handleDragEnd resize branch and the new Option-A handleDragMove resize branch would have identical bodies; @dnd-kit guarantees final dragEnd with cumulative delta; the redundant commit is idempotent — a `dispatchResizeCommit` helper extraction is a minor cleanup, not required. (4) Operator-mental-model inconsistency between Option A's live-input-update (resize) vs drag-to-move's input-lag (CSS-translate path) — flagged for operator hand-validation post-fix. (5) Process canon candidate: "@dnd-kit transform model is position-only; dimensional/rotational/skew gestures need state-mediated rendering" — substrate pattern worth canonizing for any future drag-to-rotate, drag-to-skew, drag-to-curve workflow-canvas connectors. Flagged for post-fix canon-update arc; NOT pre-locked. **Files modified**: `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-resize-live-preview.md` (new, ~1,900 words / ~250 lines markdown), `STATE.md` (this entry). **No code touched. No tests touched. No canon doc edits. The 114 unstaged screenshot deletions untouched per scope.** Active arc → none; investigation produced. Filed for next arc → **`resize-live-preview-fix`** (single combined dispatch — production handleDragMove resize branch + JSDOM keyboard test + source-shape regression gate + Playwright resize-preview spec; depends on Option A lock). After fix arc lands + operator-verifies at staging, post-fix canon-update arc considers (a) DECISIONS.md entry for @dnd-kit transform-model-asymmetry observation, (b) snap-during-resize follow-up investigation evaluation. Canon entry count unchanged at 22 pending the fix + canon-update sequence.

- **2026-05-20 — Hover-state staging-regression fix arc shipped (uncommitted)** — pointerover/pointerout via bubbling event semantics; display:contents intermediate element root-caused. Pre-flight: HEAD verified `546aa46` per process canon (read-only hover-state investigation). Operator-confirmed root cause via staging DevTools diagnostic (native pointerenter listener attached at staging — zero events across 10+ hovers): the 3 narrowed candidates in investigation `546aa46` (ancestor pointer-events:none, latent overlay, React-19/DndContext batching) were ALL ruled out; the actual cause was a fourth candidate the investigation didn't enumerate. **Root cause locked**: `onPointerEnter` / `onPointerLeave` use non-bubbling native semantics; their hit-test cascade depends on layout-box crossing; the DOM chain between operator pointer and the FreeFormPlacedWidget draggable wrapper includes an intermediate `display: contents` div emitted by the `registerComponent` HOC at `frontend/src/lib/visual-editor/registry/register.ts:215` (every visually-editable component is wrapped); `display: contents` has no layout box; the cascade breaks at it in real chromium; JSDOM ignores `display: contents` entirely + dispatches synthetic events directly to the handler element so unit tests passed. **Fix**: swap to bubbling variants `onPointerOver` / `onPointerOut`. Bubbling rides DOM-tree edges (parent/child relationships) not layout-box adjacency, so it passes through `display: contents` cleanly. **`relatedTarget` contains-check** on pointerout is load-bearing: pointerout fires whenever the pointer moves to ANY child element, NOT only on widget exit; without the check, descendant-pointer-motion would flicker isHovered → false → true. With the check, isHovered → false runs only on true widget exit. Pointerover setting isHovered → true is idempotent across repeated fires. **Playwright integration path chosen**: option (d) — inline HTML fixture via `page.setContent` + real chromium pointer events, plus a source-shape regression gate inspecting the production file via Node `readFileSync`. Rationale: options (a) staging URL, (b) local dev server with seed, (c) unskip+extend FF-7 spec all require a seeded free-form Focus template at predictable coords (FF-7 spec is `.skip`'d pending this seed). Option (d) reproduces the EXACT bug-shape (display:contents intermediate + pointer-event handlers) without infrastructure dependencies. Spec lives at `frontend/tests/e2e/focus-builder-hover-pointer-semantics.spec.ts` (~430 LOC). Production wiring continues to be covered by JSDOM vitest; the FF-7 spec activates when its seed lands. **Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied**: pre-fix Playwright result = 5 passed (fixture demonstration scenarios) + 1 FAILED (source-shape regression gate asserting production code uses `onPointerOver` / `onPointerOut` + relatedTarget contains-check — found the broken `onPointerEnter` / `onPointerLeave` instead). Post-fix Playwright result = 6/6 passing in 1.4s. The source-shape gate is the load-bearing pre-fix-fails / post-fix-passes assertion; the 4 fixture scenarios document the real-chromium behavior of the fix shape. **JSDOM tests updated** in `FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx`: 6 hover tests' event names updated (`pointerEnter` → `pointerOver`; `pointerLeave` → `pointerOut` with `relatedTarget: document.body`); test names updated; 1 NEW test added (`pointerout with relatedTarget INSIDE widget does NOT hide handles`) explicitly guarding the contains-check using `screen.getByTestId("focus-builder-placed-widget-core")` as a known descendant of the draggable wrapper. Vitest 21/21 FreeFormPlacedWidget passes post-fix. **Investigation `546aa46` corrected**: §11 (Root cause confirmed via staging diagnostic) + §12 (Process canon candidates) appended; the investigation's locked 3-candidate set documented as ruled out; the actual fourth candidate (event-type-semantic axis: bubbling vs non-bubbling) documented in detail. **Architectural surprises during build**: (1) `display: contents` semantics in chromium — `registerComponent`'s HOC wraps every visually-editable widget in a `display: contents` div for the runtime editor's click-to-edit gesture, and this wrapper is in the DOM chain on every widget render. The non-bubbling hit-test cascade interacts with `display: contents` in a way that's invisible to JSDOM but load-bearing in chromium. (2) The Playwright `getByTestId` matcher counts DOM presence not visibility — my first fixture iteration used `style="display:none"` to toggle the handles, which counted regardless; the production behavior is React conditional render (mount/unmount), so the fixture was updated to mount/unmount handles via JS DOM manipulation, mirroring the production React render contract. (3) The `display: contents` HOC was added in Phase R-1 for the runtime editor selection overlay; it's load-bearing for that feature and cannot simply be removed. The fix routes around it via event-type choice, NOT by removing the HOC. (4) The investigation locked 3 candidates by LOCATION (ancestor chain, overlay, batching) but didn't enumerate by EVENT-TYPE SEMANTICS — generalizes to: investigations of event-related bugs must include the bubbling/non-bubbling/capture/passive axis explicitly. **Post-fix canon-update arc candidate list (now 4 entries)**: (i) Q-10 selection-only refinement → "hover OR selection" (carried from prior arc); (ii) investigation source-candidate audit ("have we enumerated by every relevant axis?") gate; (iii) investigation-time UX locks should be revisited by operator-experience data (carried from prior arc); (iv) **NEW** — investigations of event-related bugs must enumerate by event-type semantics (bubbling vs non-bubbling, capture vs bubble, passive vs active, synthetic vs native) as a load-bearing axis orthogonal to location enumeration. Filed for post-fix canon-update arc per established sequencing; NOT filed in this fix arc. **Operator-observable assertion canon honored**: all Playwright fixture scenarios assert on DOM presence (via `getByTestId(...).toHaveCount(N)`) of the handle elements at their specific testids. JSDOM tests assert on `screen.getAllByTestId("focus-builder-resize-handle")` length. Source-shape gate asserts on production file regex matches. No wrapper-attribute assertions. **FF-1 through FF-7 regression surface unchanged** — all 21 FreeFormPlacedWidget vitest tests pass post-fix (drag wiring, resize handle render conditions, context menu, hover-state). **Gate cascade**: `npx tsc -b` clean; vitest run (focused) 21/21 FreeFormPlacedWidget passes; vitest run (full suite) 3161/3163 pass with 1 pre-existing failure (`Tier2TemplatesEditor.test.tsx > preview-card chrome preset updates live when chrome pill clicked` — verified pre-existing on `546aa46` HEAD pre-fix via `git stash` + full-suite re-run; passes when run in isolation; pollution / order-dependency unrelated to this fix arc — pre-fix full-suite had 3160 passed, post-fix has 3161 passed = +1 new test from the contains-check guard); `npm run build` clean in 5.54s; eslint on the 3 changed files = 2 pre-existing react-refresh errors (verified pre-existing on stash; not introduced by this fix arc); Playwright `focus-builder-hover-pointer-semantics` 6/6 passing in 1.4s. **Bundle delta**: pre-fix `6,123.23 kB` → post-fix `6,123.28 kB`. Absolute delta **+0.05 kB**; percentage delta **+0.0008%**. Effectively zero, as expected for a pure event-name swap with minor handler-body addition (the relatedTarget contains-check). **Migration head unchanged**: `r104_migrate_focus_templates_to_freeform`. **Files modified**: `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx` (~36 LOC delta: handler bodies updated + JSX prop names + comment-canon updates), `FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx` (~30 LOC delta: 6 existing hover tests updated; 1 new contains-check test added at ~46 LOC), `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-hover-state-staging-regression.md` (+~100 LOC: §11 + §12 appended), `STATE.md` (this entry). **Files added**: `frontend/tests/e2e/focus-builder-hover-pointer-semantics.spec.ts` (~430 LOC: inline fixture + 4 fixture scenarios + 1 sanity scenario + 1 source-shape regression gate). **Files NOT touched per scope discipline**: `ResizeHandleOverlay.tsx` (confirmed innocent across multiple investigations), `register.ts` (display:contents HOC stays — load-bearing for runtime editor), today-pin-widget rendering path (display:contents stays; fix routes around it via event-type choice), the 114 unstaged screenshot deletions, CLAUDE.md / PLATFORM_ARCHITECTURE.md / DESIGN_LANGUAGE.md / DECISIONS.md / BRIDGEABLE_MASTER.md / FUNERAL_HOME_VERTICAL.md / VISION.md (canon docs — canon refinement filing deferred to post-fix canon-update arc), `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-free-form-focus-canvas.md` (per prompt). **Active arc** → hover-state-staging-regression-fix (this arc; uncommitted). **Filed for next arc** → post-fix canon-update arc considers DECISIONS.md entries for the 4 candidates listed above. - **2026-05-20 (later evening) — Read-only investigation arc produced: `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-hover-state-staging-regression.md` filed (uncommitted); locks test-substrate gap; root cause unlocked pending DevTools diagnostic; fix arc shape locked.** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `a1c10c7` per process canon (fix arc — resize-handle UX refinements). Investigation triggered by operator-verification regression at staging after `a1c10c7` deployed: Finding 1 hover-state FAILS in real browser ("They don't appear upon hover"); selection still works. JSDOM vitest 350/350 had passed pre-deploy including five new hover-state tests at `FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx:424-543`. Scope: Finding 1 only (Finding 2 UUID leak not yet operator-verified at staging; deferred). **Static-code audit covered**: `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx`, `PlacedWidgetCore.tsx`, `ResizeHandleOverlay.tsx`, `WidgetFreeFormLayer.tsx`, `FocusBuilderCanvas.tsx` outer wrapper, `FocusBuilderPage.tsx` DragOverlay/sensor config, `@dnd-kit/core` type declarations + PointerSensor source. **Six hypotheses audited (A spread overwrite / B child absorption / C non-bubbling / D CSS layout / E StrictMode / F multiple draggables)**. Hypothesis A ruled out doubly — handlers correctly ordered AFTER spread per FF-4 canon at `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx:198-207`, AND `DraggableAttributes` type at `node_modules/@dnd-kit/core/dist/hooks/useDraggable.d.ts:14-21` is purely ARIA-shaped (no pointer enter/leave handlers in `attributes`); `PointerSensor.activators` at `dist/sensors/pointer/PointerSensor.d.ts:10` is `onPointerDown` only (no pointer enter/leave in `listeners`). Hypothesis B ruled out — PlacedWidgetCore has no pointer handlers + no `pointer-events: none`. Hypothesis E ruled out — production build doesn't double-invoke; would fire twice not zero times. Hypothesis F ruled out — cascade is downstream of failing path. Hypothesis D ruled out at focus-builder layer; cannot rule out at ancestor chain without DevTools. **Hypothesis C confirmed in refined framing** — narrow form ("pointerenter non-bubbling") doesn't hold at W3C spec level (pointerenter fires on ancestor when entered via descendant); refined form does hold: `fireEvent.pointerEnter(draggable)` is a synchronous synthetic React event dispatch that bypasses every layer of browser hit-testing, compositing, native event delivery. **Tests prove handler-if-fired only; do NOT prove handler-fires**. **Root cause NOT locked from static evidence alone** — first FF-series investigation in this arc where static-code audit was exhausted without conclusive file:line evidence. Candidate set narrowed to three (in likelihood order): (1) ancestor `pointer-events: none` somewhere above the focus-builder canvas in the admin layout chrome / global stylesheets — JSDOM doesn't compute CSS so silently passes; (2) latent overlay element absolutely positioned over canvas that intercepts hit testing; (3) React 19 batching / DndContext re-render interaction. DevTools diagnostic step against staging required to discriminate. **Test-substrate gap locked independent of root cause**: all 5 hover-state JSDOM tests share the identical `fireEvent.pointerEnter(draggable) → expect handles` pattern; none of them assert hit-testable surface, ancestor `pointer-events`, layout compositing, or native event delivery. The `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx:50-52` Q-40 comment already acknowledges JSDOM pointer-event unreliability for *drag gestures* via PointerSensor; the `a1c10c7` fix arc extended a NEW pointer-event surface (pointerenter/pointerleave outside @dnd-kit's listeners) WITHOUT applying the Q-40 discipline — covered only by JSDOM unit tests, no Playwright spec. **Fix shape locked**: single combined fix arc, sequenced internally — (a) DevTools diagnostic against staging as first step (no commit); (b) write Playwright spec FIRST in `frontend/tests/e2e/` covering hover-in → handles → hover-out → no-handles; (c) confirm spec FAILS against `a1c10c7` HEAD per verify-against-pre-fix canon; (d) apply production-code fix (LOC depends on which §4 candidate is real — 1-3 LOC if ancestor pointer-events override, 5-20 LOC if overlay interception, 30-60 LOC if React-batching refactor); (e) confirm Playwright passes + vitest 5 hover tests unchanged; (f) commit. Total fix-arc LOC estimate: **~55-160 LOC**, dominated by Playwright spec (~50-100) over production code (~5-60). **Process canon candidate filed**: "Unit tests using `fireEvent.<pointer-event>` prove handler-if-fired only; new pointer-event surfaces require Playwright coverage before merge. The Q-40 narrow lock generalizes to ALL pointer-event surfaces in the focus builder, not just drag-gesture PointerSensor events." Recommend filing in post-fix canon-update arc, not in the fix arc itself. Optional second canon candidate: "staging operator verification is the canonical real-browser gate, not vitest's JSDOM" — broader applicability. **Architectural surprises during investigation**: (1) `useDraggable.attributes` is purely ARIA-shaped — FF-4 plumbing canon was correctly applied but addressed a problem that doesn't exist at this surface (no harm; canon-driven defensive coding is free when not needed); (2) JSDOM's lack of CSS / layout silently undermines a class of UI behavior tests broader than Q-40's narrow scope; (3) all 5 hover-state tests share an identical pattern that doesn't distinguish "the handler fired" from "the handler did the right thing when fired"; (4) the investigation could not lock root cause from static evidence alone — first such instance in the FF-series; honest accounting flagged in §10 of the doc. **Files**: `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-hover-state-staging-regression.md` (new, ~2,400 words / ~280 lines markdown), `STATE.md` (this entry). **No code touched. No tests touched. No canon doc edits.** Active arc → none; investigation produced. Filed for next arc → **`hover-state-staging-fix`** (combined production-code fix + Playwright spec; depends on DevTools diagnostic as first step). After fix arc lands + operator-verifies at staging, post-fix canon-update arc considers `DECISIONS.md` entry for Q-40 generalization + investigation-cannot-lock-from-static-alone meta-canon. Canon entry count unchanged at 22 pending the fix + canon-update sequence.

- **2026-05-20 — Resize handle UX refinements fix arc shipped (uncommitted) — Finding 1 (hover-state) + Finding 2 (DragOverlay UUID leak class-fix).** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `224cc06` per process canon (read-only investigation commit). Single combined dispatch against locks in `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-resize-handle-ux-refinements.md`. **Finding 1 — hover-state addition**: `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx` gained local `isHovered` state + `onPointerEnter` / `onPointerLeave` handlers (declared AFTER `{...attributes}` spread per FF-4 plumbing canon so @dnd-kit's attributes can't overwrite). Resize handle render condition changed from `selected ? <ResizeHandleOverlay/> : null` → `(isHovered || selected || isDragging) ? <ResizeHandleOverlay/> : null`. The `isDragging` defensive third branch was added pre-emptively (not via runtime verification) because @dnd-kit pointer-capture behavior during keyboard-sensor active drag is environment-sensitive; the cost is zero (one boolean read) and the risk removed is handles-vanishing-mid-resize. Touch / pointer-coarse degrades naturally via selection branch (no special-case code). **Finding 2 — UUID leak class-fix via `resolveDragLabel` pure helper**: new `resolveDragLabel.ts` (~54 LOC) + `resolveDragLabel.test.ts` (9 tests covering all four drag-id shapes). Helper encapsulates palette-prefix check directly (Option B per dispatch — no cross-file dependency on `FocusBuilderPalette.tsx::paletteItemIdToSlug`; both files own a copy of the canonical `palette-widget:` prefix string). FocusBuilderPage.tsx's `handleDragStart` callsite at line 792 changed from `setActiveDragLabel(slug ?? id)` → `setActiveDragLabel(resolveDragLabel(id))`. Returns palette slug for `palette-widget:<slug>` ids (preserves existing operator-visible label for palette drags); returns null for all other shapes (DragOverlay child guard at line 1303 short-circuits cleanly — no refinement needed). The class-of-bug fix extended to whole-widget drag (FF-3) automatically — the `free-form-placed-widget:<uuid>` shape was leaking too but operators hadn't reported it because the prefix made it read as a label, not a UUID. **Architectural surprise during build — load-bearing dual purpose of `activeDragLabel`**: pre-fix, `activeDragLabel !== null` at FocusBuilderPage.tsx:721 was acting as a **drag-in-progress sentinel** for the page-level arrow-key nudge guard. With my null-for-resize change, the sentinel evaporated → page-level keydown handler raced @dnd-kit's KeyboardSensor → 3 FF-4 resize integration tests failed with deterministic position drift (x=102 vs expected 100, x=194 vs expected 200, etc — the page-level nudge handler was applying its `stepDelta=1` shift on top of @dnd-kit's keyboard step). **Fix**: separated concerns with a new `isDragInProgress: boolean` state, set true in `handleDragStart`, cleared in `handleDragEnd` + `handleDragCancel`. The nudge guard now reads `isDragInProgress` instead of `activeDragLabel !== null`. Two independent signals for two independent concerns: label content (rendering decision) + drag lifecycle (event-conflict guard). The investigation flagged the DragOverlay rendering as Finding 2's source but did NOT surface this secondary usage of `activeDragLabel`; it was discovered during build via FF-4 regression test triage. **Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied**: reverting the callsite to `setActiveDragLabel(paletteItemIdToSlug(id) ?? id)` made Test B (resize-handle drag) + Test C (whole-widget drag) fail with visible UUID text in the DragOverlay; Test A (palette drag) continued passing (palette slug is the one shape both pre/post-fix render correctly). Restored → all three pass. **Test surface**: `resolveDragLabel.test.ts` (9 new tests: palette slug return, multi-segment slug, resize handle null × 2, free-form whole-widget null, bare UUID null, empty string null, palette-prefix-only edge case, unrecognized shape null); `FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx` (5 new tests covering hover-on-not-selected, hover-AND-selected, pointerleave-preserves-when-selected, pointerleave-hides-when-not-selected, touch-fallback-via-selected); `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` (3 new integration tests under new `describe("DragOverlay UUID leak class-fix")` block: Test A palette label preserved, Test B resize-handle suppressed, Test C whole-widget suppressed). All tests use the operator-observable assertion canon — assert against the rendered DOM at the specific `focus-builder-drag-overlay` testid + `focus-builder-resize-handle` testid presence/absence, NOT against wrapper attributes. **@dnd-kit aria-live announcer noted in test comments**: @dnd-kit emits a `DndLiveRegion-*` element that DOES carry the drag id ("Picked up draggable item …") for screen-reader a11y. That element is positioned-fixed + clipped to 1px (NOT operator-visible). Tests target the operator-visible DragOverlay testid, NOT the screen-reader region — initial test assertions used `queryByText(/-handle-/)` which incorrectly matched the live region; tightened to `queryByTestId("focus-builder-drag-overlay")`. **Operator-observable canon honored**: every assertion targets the specific rendered element via testid; no wrapper-attribute assertions. **Gate cascade**: 350/350 focus-builder vitest tests green (29 test files); `npx tsc -b` clean; `npm run lint` unchanged at 584 errors (all pre-existing per pre-fix diff confirmation — no new lint regressions introduced by my files); `npm run build` clean in 5.10s. **Bundle delta**: pre-arc `6,122.99 kB` → post-arc `6,123.23 kB`. Absolute delta **+0.24 kB**; percentage delta **+0.0039%**. Cost-of-fix is essentially free (one new boolean state + 54-line helper file). **Migration head unchanged**: `r104_migrate_focus_templates_to_freeform`. **LOC delta** (focus-builder only): +475 source/test modifications + 117 new file lines = ~592 LOC. Within combined-arc estimate (140-270 LOC source + tests; combined is higher because the actual cost includes the `isDragInProgress` discovery + extensive hover-state test coverage + DragOverlay class-fix integration test scaffolding). **Q-10 refinement canon entry filing**: deferred per investigation §4 — file AFTER this fix arc commits. Q-10's investigation-time lock ("8 resize handles on-selection-only") refined by this fix arc to "hover OR selection OR isDragging." Canon-update arc considers a `DECISIONS.md` entry covering both (a) the Q-10 refinement itself and (b) the discovered process canon (investigation-time UX locks may need operator-experience refinement; investigation-time source-candidate locks may miss secondary load-bearing usages of the same state). The activeDragLabel dual-purpose discovery is itself a process-canon candidate. **Files modified**: `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/components/focus-builder/FocusBuilderPage.tsx` (37 LOC delta — import + 2 new lines in handleDragStart + 1 new line in handleDragEnd + 1 new line in handleDragCancel + isDragInProgress useState + 1-line guard change at line 721 + deps array change), `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx` (43 LOC delta — import-type → import + useState + 2 useCallback handlers + 2 new wrapper props + render-condition expansion + comment updates), `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` (+239 LOC — describe block with 3 integration tests), `FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx` (+167 LOC — 5 hover-state tests + existing test rename to clarify "AND not hovered"), `resolveDragLabel.ts` (new, 54 LOC), `resolveDragLabel.test.ts` (new, 63 LOC). **Files NOT touched per scope discipline**: `ResizeHandleOverlay.tsx` (confirmed innocent during investigation), `FocusBuilderPalette.tsx::paletteItemIdToSlug` (not refactored — `resolveDragLabel` is independent), the 2 investigation docs (read-only reference), CLAUDE.md / PLATFORM_ARCHITECTURE.md / DESIGN_LANGUAGE.md / DECISIONS.md / BRIDGEABLE_MASTER.md / FUNERAL_HOME_VERTICAL.md / VISION.md (canon docs — Q-10 canon refinement filing deferred to post-deploy verification arc per investigation §4). **Active arc** → resize-handle-ux-fixes (this arc; uncommitted). **Filed for next arc** → Q-10 canon refinement entry in DECISIONS.md + investigation-arc-to-fix-arc process-canon entry capturing the `activeDragLabel` dual-purpose discovery. - **2026-05-20 (evening) — Read-only investigation arc produced: `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-resize-handle-ux-refinements.md` filed (uncommitted); locks two FF-4 operator-experience refinements; fix arc pending dispatch.** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `9e47a3e` per process canon (focus-template free-form migration arc). Investigation triggered by two operator concerns surfaced during FF-series staging verification: (1) handles should appear on hover (current Q-10 lock: selection-only) — operator feedback verbatim "I would like it to work on hover without clicking the widget if that is possible"; (2) visible UUID text adjacent to widgets during active resize drag matching `<placement-uuid>-handle-<position>`. **Finding 1 locked at option (a) — hover OR selection.** Reasoning: discoverability via hover preserves the Figma / Sketch precedent operator behavior; selection-based persistence preserves the active-manipulation case where pointer drifts off mid-resize; touch / pointer-coarse devices degrade naturally via tap-to-select. LOC est ~30-60 (local useState + pointer-enter / pointer-leave on existing draggable wrapper at `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx:170-206`; condition change at `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx:225`). **Finding 2 locked at root cause: DragOverlay rendering `activeDragLabel` (= raw drag id) for non-palette drag-id shapes.** File:line evidence: `FocusBuilderPage.tsx:792` (`setActiveDragLabel(slug ?? id)` — explicit fallback to raw id when `paletteItemIdToSlug` returns null) + `FocusBuilderPage.tsx:1312` (`{activeDragLabel}` rendered as visible text content inside the DragOverlay child at lines 1302-1315). The text appears "outside the widget's right edge" because @dnd-kit's DragOverlay follows the cursor — during resize-SE-handle drag, cursor is at bottom-right corner of widget, overlay renders adjacent. ResizeHandleOverlay confirmed innocent — every line read at `ResizeHandleOverlay.tsx:160-188`, handle divs render NO text content; data-attributes only. Same bug class affects whole-widget drag id (`free-form-placed-widget:<uuid>`) but operator hadn't reported it because the prefix made the leak look like a label rather than a raw UUID. **Fix shape**: new pure helper `resolveDragLabel(id: string): string | null` that returns slug for `palette-widget:` prefix; null for `free-form-placed-widget:` prefix; null for `<uuid>-handle-<position>` shape; null for unrecognized ids (safe default — no UUID leak by accident). DragOverlay child guard at line 1303 already handles null correctly. LOC est ~40-80 (helper + handler change + 6-10 unit tests + 1 integration test). **Combined fix arc shape recommendation: single dispatch** — both findings touch the same FF-4 substrate; ~140-270 LOC total; no architectural dependency between them. **Q-10 refinement note flagged**: substrate now carries operator-experience-derived knowledge that the Q-10 investigation-time lock (selection-only) needs refinement to hover-OR-selection. Canon-update arc should file AFTER the fix arc commits, recording both the new behavior and the investigation-time → operator-time refinement chain. **Architectural surprises**: (a) the same bug class affects ALL non-palette drag-id shapes, not just resize handles; (b) `paletteItemIdToSlug` was never designed as a universal label resolver and the `slug ?? id` fallback was a load-bearing safety net that started leaking when FF-4 introduced the resize-handle id shape; (c) ResizeHandleOverlay is genuinely innocent; (d) Q-10 predates operator hands; (e) DragOverlay is net-positive for one drag-id shape (palette) and net-negative for two (whole-widget, resize-handle) — suppressing via null return for the latter two preserves the overlay component for any future drag shapes that need a floating label. **Step 4 evidence conclusive** — no live-DOM DevTools diagnostic step required for the fix arc; dispatch directly against locked source candidate. **Files modified**: `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-resize-handle-ux-refinements.md` (new, ~2,400 words / ~280 lines markdown), `STATE.md` (this entry). **No code touched. No tests. No canon doc edits.** Active arc → none; investigation produced. Filed for next arc → **`resize-handle-ux-fixes`** (combined fix for Findings 1 + 2; depends on locks above). After fix arc lands, canon-update arc considers a `DECISIONS.md` entry for the Q-10 refinement + the discovered process canon (investigation-time UX locks refined by operator experience). Canon entry count unchanged at 22.

- **2026-05-20 — Focus template free-form migration arc shipped (uncommitted) — Standalone data-migration arc; reverses investigation Q-24 as product decision.** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `14844c6` (FF-7). Standalone scope: NO substrate changes, NO frontend code changes, NO new canon entries. Single Alembic data migration `r104_migrate_focus_templates_to_freeform` (~315 LOC including pure helpers + 36-test coverage file at `backend/tests/test_focus_template_freeform_migration.py` — ~480 LOC, all green). Converts all grid-shape Focus templates in the `focus_templates` table to free-form-shape placements matching the Decide canvas substrate shipped in FF-1 through FF-7. **Q-24 reversal rationale**: at investigation time, decoupling substrate landing from migration risk was correct. Now that substrate has landed, the product decision is clear — Focus templates ARE Decide canvas substrate; existing grid-shape templates should match. **Per-placement translation rules**: widget placements get `x = starting_column * (canvas_width / 12)`, `width = column_span * (canvas_width / 12)`, `y = row_index * 200`, `height = 200` (universal fallback — widget registry's `defaultDimensions` lives frontend-side per F-3 substrate; backend has no access at Alembic time + no need; operators adjust heights post-migration via FF-4's resize gesture), `z_index = 0`. Inherited core placements (`is_core: true`) use the Q-20 canonical formula: `core_width = canvas_width * (clamped_column_span / 12)`, `core_x = (canvas_width - core_width) / 2`, `core_y = 40`, `core_height = canvas_height - 40`. The migration reads `default_column_span` from the placement's stored `column_span` (not from the live `focus_cores` row) because the F-series validator already enforces that `is_core` placements match the inherited core's component identity, and authors typically set `column_span == default_column_span` — self-contained migration discipline beats cross-table joins for no behavioral difference. **Canvas dimensions stamped per FF-1 pattern**: templates without `canvas_config.width` / `.height` get the FF-1 defaults (1200×800). Pre-existing canvas_config keys (gap_size, background_treatment, padding, etc.) are preserved verbatim — partial canvas_config blobs survive the stamp. **Grid fields cleared post-migration**: each placement loses `starting_column` + `column_span`; rows lose `column_count`. **Idempotent both directions**: upgrade detects already-free-form templates via field-presence check on any of x/y/width/height (matches backend `_placement_shape` semantics) and skips with explanatory log line; downgrade detects already-grid templates via the inverse check + skips. **Reversible**: down migration restores grid shape with `column_count: 12` per row + derived `starting_column` / `column_span` via rounding `x / (canvas_width / 12)` and `width / (canvas_width / 12)`. Provided for emergency rollback only; never expected to fire. **Investigation findings surfaced during pre-flight**: (1) The only currently seeded template `scheduling-fh` (vertical=manufacturing) ships with `rows: []` — accessories are populated via Tier 3 (`focus_compositions`) sub-arc C, not via Tier 2 placements. Migration on the dev DB found 0 templates (empty `focus_templates` table verified via psql); migration on staging will see 1 active row with empty rows and trivially skip-or-no-op (no placements to convert). **Operator-authored templates** are the real migration target — any operator who used the F-3 builder to author grid-shape templates before this arc shipped gets their data lifted to the canvas substrate without manual re-authoring. (2) `is_core: bool` is an EXPLICIT discriminator on placements per the `FocusTemplate` model docstring at `backend/app/models/focus_template.py:34`. Service-layer validator enforces exactly-one `is_core: true` placement per template + identity match against the inherited core. No fallback needed; explicit field carries the signal. (3) `column_count` lives on the ROW envelope (1..12) — rows can have arbitrary column counts in F-series, NOT always 12. The migration uses canvas-relative arithmetic (`canvas_width / 12`) regardless of `column_count` because the FF canvas substrate is canvas-relative, not row-relative; this is a deliberate semantic shift documented in FF-1's `_freeform_row` test fixture comment ("column_count is irrelevant for free-form placements but the row-level validator still requires it"). (4) Backend has NO widget-registry access at Alembic time — registry is frontend-only per F-3 substrate. Universal 200px height fallback is the only sensible value at migration time. Operators adjust via FF-4's resize gesture post-deploy. (5) JSONB read/write at Alembic time goes through `op.get_bind()` + `sa.text("CAST(:rows AS jsonb)")` with `json.dumps` parameter values — matches the pattern in adjacent migrations for raw JSONB UPDATE. Reads handled via `_coerce_jsonb` helper that defensively handles dict/list/string driver variations. **Test coverage** (36 tests, 1.35s wall, all green): shape detection × 6 (free-form-via-x, grid-via-starting_column, empty rows, empty placements, free-form-via-width, defensive non-dict row); free-form migration × 9 (widget translation basic + offset + row_index, clears-grid-fields, row loses column_count, core uses Q-20 full-width-centered + narrower-centered, preserves prop_overrides + display_config + placement_id, mixed widget+core in two rows); canvas stamping × 5 (empty, None, partial preserves keys, explicit dimensions preserved, only-width stamps height); to-grid downgrade × 4 (widget reverse, row regains column_count, round-trip restores grid, clamps overflow when x+width round to span > 12); idempotency × 4 (upgrade skips already-freeform, upgrade twice no-op, downgrade skips already-grid, downgrade skips empty); defensive × 3 (non-dict row passes through, non-dict placement passes through, missing starting_column defaults to 0); JSONB coercion × 4 (dict, list, string, None); end-to-end DB × 1 (seed a FocusCore + grid-shape FocusTemplate via service layer, run migration pure-function path against the live row via connection bind, verify post-row carries free-form shape + Q-20 core + canvas stamped + column_count stripped + gap_size preserved). **Gate cascade**: 36/36 migration-specific tests green; 110/110 across `test_focus_template_inheritance_service.py` + `test_focus_template_freeform_validation.py` + `test_focus_compositions.py` + new migration test file (no regression in adjacent F-series tests); `alembic upgrade head` clean (migration applied: `migrated=0 skipped=0 total=0` on empty dev DB); `alembic downgrade -1` clean (`reverted=0 skipped=0 total=0`); re-`upgrade head` clean (full cycle idempotency confirmed); `npx tsc -b` clean (no frontend changes). **Migration head advances**: `r103_focus_templates_edit_session` → `r104_migrate_focus_templates_to_freeform`. **Frontend code unchanged.** **Architectural surprises during build, in order of significance:** (1) **`column_count` per-row vs canvas-relative ambiguity** — the F-series schema permits arbitrary `column_count` 1..12 per row, but the FF canvas substrate is canvas-relative (always /12 against canvas_width). The migration deliberately treats all grid-shape templates as if column_count=12 for x/width arithmetic, because (a) the seeded scheduling-fh template uses column_count=12 throughout, (b) the inherited core's `default_column_span` validator caps at 12, (c) any operator-authored template with column_count<12 would still convert sensibly (the placement just won't span the full canvas width post-migration, matching its grid-shape proportional position). Documented inline in the migration helper. (2) **Self-contained migration discipline beat cross-table joins** — the inherited core's `default_column_span` lives on `focus_cores` (Tier 1), but the migration reads from the placement's stored `column_span` instead. Rationale: F-series authors set `column_span == default_column_span` by convention (validator enforces identity match on `is_core: true`); avoiding the join means the migration is self-contained + easier to reason about + has no risk of an out-of-band `focus_cores` change mid-deploy invalidating in-progress migrations. (3) **JSONB driver variance forced a `_coerce_jsonb` helper** — depending on psycopg2 version + connection state, JSONB columns may come back as native Python dict/list OR as string. The helper normalizes; tested explicitly with 4 cases. (4) **Test discovery via importlib bypassed Alembic's import mechanism** — Alembic migration files aren't importable via dotted-path because `backend/alembic/versions/` lacks `__init__.py`. Tests load the migration module via `importlib.util.spec_from_file_location` against the absolute path. Pattern is reusable for any future migration tests that need to exercise pure-function helpers. **Manual verification deferred to post-deploy on staging**: load `scheduling-fh` template in admin; confirm canvas renders via WidgetFreeFormLayer (per FF-2 canvas substrate mode detection); FF-3 drag, FF-4 resize, FF-5 z-index, FF-6 inspector positioning, FF-7 snap/marquee/align gestures all work against the migrated data. Local dev DB has 0 focus_templates rows (verified via psql query) — staging is the first surface where real seeded data flows through the migration. **Future arcs**: if operator-authored Tier 2 templates accumulate in production AND a column_count<12 row shape appears, audit migration output for those edge cases. Pure-helper test fixtures cover column_count=12 only; staging deploy is the first real-data verification.

- **2026-05-20 — Sub-arc FF-7 shipped (uncommitted) — FF-series ARC FINALE — Snap-to-alignment + keyboard nudge + multi-select on canvas + Playwright pointer-event gate.** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `065b59e` (FF-6). FF-7 closes the FF-series investigation (Q-1–Q-37 LOCKED) and mitigates the three pinned risks (Q-38 deploy-race, Q-39 canvas-dimension overflow, Q-40 JSDOM-vs-pointer-events gap). The free-form Focus canvas substrate is now FEATURE-COMPLETE; future Focus authoring work moves into vertical-specific arcs (real widget functionality, generation Focus templates per BRIDGEABLE_MASTER §3.26.11.12). **Four concerns shipped in one arc, each ringfenced to a self-contained subsystem:** (1) **Snap-to-alignment helpers** per Q-11 (b): new pure helper `computeSnapAdjustment` (261 LOC + 213 LOC test) computes proximity-to-6px against other placements' left/right/center edges + canvas centerlines; Alt-key disables; multi-axis snap allowed; SnapLine emit. New `SnapLineOverlay` component (72 LOC + 81 LOC test) renders 1px brass-accent overlay lines spanning the canvas with `pointer-events: none`. Page-level `handleDragMove` (DragMoveEvent from @dnd-kit) wires live snap during drag; `handleDragEnd` applies snap AFTER canvas-bounds clamp, then RE-clamps so a snap target near the edge that would push outside defers to the bound. Document-level keydown/keyup track alt-key state in `altKeyHeldRef` (ref-as-dominant-defense per the 2026-05-19 canon — @dnd-kit's DragMoveEvent does not expose activator modifiers mid-gesture). Snap lines cleared at drag-end + drag-cancel. (2) **Keyboard nudge** per Q-12: window-level keydown handler in FocusBuilderPage. Arrow keys nudge selected widget(s) by 1px; Shift+arrow nudges by 10px; `]` / `[` move z-order forward/backward; Shift+`]` / Shift+`[` move to front/back. Z-order shortcuts SINGLE-SELECT only per investigation (multi-select z-order behavior undefined; deferred). Defensive guards: ignores typing in INPUT / TEXTAREA / contenteditable / BUTTON (covers ScrubbableButton's own arrow-driven scrub UX) AND ignores when `activeDragLabel !== null` (a drag is in flight; @dnd-kit's KeyboardSensor owns arrow keys). Both guards were verify-against-pre-fix-required — the F-3.1b / F-3.1c chrome-scrub regression tests + FF-4 resize tests failed when my window listener hijacked their ArrowRight events; adding the BUTTON + activeDragLabel guards restored every previously-green test. (3) **Multi-select on canvas** per Q-16 (a) + Q-17 (b) + Q-18 (a): `FocusBuilderSelectionContext` extended additively with `widgets-multi` discriminator + five helpers (`addToSelection` / `removeFromSelection` / `clearSelection` / `setMultiSelection` / `isInSelection`). Single-select model UNCHANGED. PlacedWidgetCore extended with optional `onShiftSelect` prop — when present, shift+click routes through it (calls `addToSelection` or `removeFromSelection` depending on `isInSelection`); regular click still calls `onSelect` (preserves F-3.1c behavior). New `MarqueeOverlay` (57 LOC + 75 LOC test): absolutely-positioned rubber-band rectangle with 1px brass-accent border + ~15% alpha brass-subtle fill; 3×3 px threshold before rendering. WidgetFreeFormLayer accepts `onLayerPointerDown` / `Move` / `Up` props + carries `data-canvas-background="true"` on the layer element — page-level marquee dispatcher discriminates pointer-down by `target.getAttribute("data-canvas-background")` so a pointer-down on the canvas background starts marquee, but pointer-down on a widget starts widget-drag (gestures route to different state machines via target attribute, not via stopPropagation arms-race). On pointer-up, marquee state computes AABB intersection of every free-form placement vs the marquee rect; `setMultiSelection(intersectingIds)` commits the selection. Marquee below the 3px threshold collapses to `clearSelection` (background-click semantics preserved). **Critical fix during build: the pre-FF-7 hook `updateWidget` read `rowsRef.current` synchronously BEFORE calling `setRowsDraft(next)`; rowsRef is updated by a useEffect that runs AFTER render, so two synchronous `updateWidget` calls (e.g., multi-select arrow nudge moving widgets A + B) raced — the second call read the OLD rowsRef value and silently OVERWROTE the first call's setRowsDraft. The fix: convert to functional `setRowsDraft((current) => ...)` so React's batched-state-update pipeline supplies each call with the latest state. queueSave fires unconditionally on every call (debounced save coalesces; saving unchanged state is harmless at the boundary). Six existing F-3 / FF-3 / FF-4 / FF-5 / FF-6 hook regression tests stay green with the functional updater (verified). This is the most architecturally interesting change in FF-7 because it surfaces a latent race in updateWidget that was undetectable before multi-select made sequential same-tick mutations a load-bearing path.** New `computeAlignTargets` pure helper (79 LOC + 89 LOC test): six align actions (left / right / center-horizontal / top / bottom / center-vertical) over the selection bounding box (NOT canvas — operator intent is "align THESE widgets to each other"). New `AlignInspectorSection` (107 LOC + 81 LOC test): 2×3 button grid in the inspector, brass-accent hover, lucide AlignStartVertical / AlignCenterVertical / etc. icons; disabled when `selectedPlacements.length < 2`; multi-select count caption underneath. **CanvasContextMenu extended with `actionSet` prop** (default "z-order" preserves FF-5; new "align" branch renders the 6 align icons with `context-menu-action-align-${action}` test-ids); page-level dispatcher passes `actionSet={selection.kind === "widgets-multi" ? "align" : "z-order"}` and unified `handleContextMenuActionUnified` routes the action vocabulary by selection.kind. FocusBuilderInspector branches on `selection.kind === "widgets-multi"` BEFORE the single-select widget branch: hides Configuration / Placement / Chrome / Position / Layer / Remove; shows ONLY AlignInspectorSection per Q-18 (a). Cleanly composed onto existing F-2 inspector. (4) **Playwright pointer-event verification gate** per Q-40: new spec file `frontend/tests/e2e/focus-builder-freeform.spec.ts` (207 LOC) with 5 chromium scenarios covering pointer drag, pointer resize SE handle, focus-preservation-during-canvas-drag (FF-6 load-bearing UX correctness), snap visual feedback, marquee selection. Spec body fully written; scenarios marked `.skip` pending two staging-side seed gaps (a free-form-template fixture + a canonical URL path opening the Focus Builder against it). Activation is a one-line per-scenario change once the seed lands. CI integration NOT yet wired into `.github/workflows/playwright-staging.yml` (which currently runs only `tests/e2e/runtime-editor/`); extending that workflow OR adding a sibling workflow is a deferred follow-up. Total touched: ~2,912 LOC. **Tests shipped Phase FF-7**: 333/333 focus-builder + hook tests passing (+57 vs FF-6: +12 computeSnapAdjustment + 5 SnapLineOverlay + 9 computeAlignTargets + 4 AlignInspectorSection + 5 MarqueeOverlay + 9 FocusBuilderSelectionContext + 3 PlacedWidgetCore shift-click + 3 CanvasContextMenu actionSet + 3 FocusBuilderInspector multi-select + 4 FocusBuilderPage integration). **Playwright spec: 5 scenarios registered, 5 skipped pending staging seed; spec body complete and exercises real chromium pointer pipeline once activated.** **tsc clean.** **eslint clean for FF-7 net change** — 584 / 473 errors / 111 warnings post-FF-7 EXACTLY matches the pre-FF-7 (FF-6) baseline; no new warnings or errors introduced. The pre-existing react-refresh/only-export-components warnings on FocusBuilderCanvas / FreeFormPlacedWidget / PlacedWidgetCore / FocusBuilderSelectionContext are inherited patterns, not FF-7-introduced. **vite build clean** (5.43s); bundle **6,122.99 kB** vs FF-6 baseline **6,107.89 kB** = **+15.10 kB absolute / +0.247% percentage** (separately reported per F-3.1c precedent; well within ±0.5% tolerance). Backend pytest unchanged — FF-7 touches zero backend files. **Architectural surprises during build, in order of significance:** (1) **The hook updateWidget race surfaced ONLY when multi-select made sequential same-tick mutations load-bearing** — the latent bug had existed since F-3 (or earlier) but was always masked because F-3's single-widget mutations or FF-3's single-drag commits never queued two `updateWidget` calls in the same JS tick. Converting to functional setState was a 30-line surgical fix preserving all existing behavior. The pattern's discovery itself is the most architecturally interesting moment of FF-7 — the multi-select feature literally exposed pre-FF-7 latent timing fragility, and the fix is now load-bearing for ANY future arc that calls updateWidget multiple times synchronously. (2) **Keyboard-nudge listener hijack of ScrubbableButton + @dnd-kit KeyboardSensor** — first runs of FF-7 broke 5 pre-existing tests (F-3.1b chrome scrub × 2, FF-4 resize × 3) because my window-keydown listener processed arrow keys before the inner consumer-component handlers. Fix: add `tag === "BUTTON"` short-circuit (covers ScrubbableButton + LayerInspectorSection buttons + AlignInspectorSection buttons + tab buttons) + `activeDragLabel !== null` short-circuit (covers active @dnd-kit gestures). Both guards are minimal AND test-validated; the regression test set caught both issues immediately. (3) **Marquee pointer-up captured stale React synthetic-event reference** — initial implementation called `(e.currentTarget as HTMLElement).getBoundingClientRect()` INSIDE the `setMarquee((prev) => ...)` updater body; React pools synthetic events, so by the time the updater function runs, `e.currentTarget` is null. Fix: capture rect + coords OUTSIDE the updater (before the call), close over the captured values inside. (4) **The selection.kind="widgets-multi" inspector branch sits BEFORE the single-select widget branch** in FocusBuilderInspector — the order matters because both branches handle `mode === "template"`; multi-select must short-circuit before the single-widget findPlacementById path runs. Documented in the inspector source comment block. (5) **Drag-of-non-selected-widget UX decision: deferred — only-this-widget moves on multi-select-active state** — the FF-7 prompt acknowledged the ambiguity; I chose Figma precedent (a drag of a widget NOT in the multi-selection moves only that widget; selection persists). Documented in the FreeFormPlacedWidget drag flow + future-polish flags below. **Build-report item answers** (per FF-7 prompt's 13-item gate): (1) Snap composed cleanly with FF-3 drag substrate; snap fires AFTER canvas-bounds clamp; snap result re-clamped so a snap target near the edge defers to the bound. (2) Keyboard nudge correctly preventsDefault on arrows + bails on BUTTON activeElement + bails when activeDragLabel != null; ScrubbableButton + @dnd-kit KeyboardSensor regression tests stay green. (3) Multi-select state extension composed cleanly with single-select; addToSelection idempotent across single / multi / none cases; isInSelection works across single + multi. (4) Marquee AABB intersection handles fully-inside, partial overlap, and below-threshold + click-without-drag-clears-selection cases (verified via integration test). (5) AlignInspectorSection's selection-bounding-box align computation matches operator intent — align-left targets `min(x)`, right targets `max(x+width)-width`, center-horizontal targets bbox-center. Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied at integration level on Test A (multi-select via shift+click + align). (6) CanvasContextMenu's `actionSet` prop composed cleanly with FF-5 single-select action set; the actionSet="align" branch renders the 6 lucide AlignXXX icons via the same MenuItem array pattern; data-action-set attribute exposes the active vocabulary for assertion targeting. (7) Playwright config + spec consumed the EXISTING `frontend/playwright.config.ts` infrastructure (testDir `tests/e2e/`, chromium project). Spec file lives at `tests/e2e/focus-builder-freeform.spec.ts` OUTSIDE the runtime-editor subdir; CI integration deferred — the existing `.github/workflows/playwright-staging.yml` runs only `tests/e2e/runtime-editor/` and adding the focus-builder spec requires a workflow-extension follow-up. Scenarios are fully implemented and ready to activate via a one-line per-scenario edit when the seed lands. NOT internal wrapper attributes. (11) Bundle delta +15.10 kB absolute / +0.247% percentage (separately reported). Risks Q-38 (deploy race) mitigated by FF-1-before-FF-2 sequential dispatch (shipped). - **2026-05-20 — Sub-arc FF-6 shipped (uncommitted) — Inspector positioning fields (X / Y / Width / Height) with uncontrolled-with-sync focus-preservation pattern (fourth operator-interactive FF sub-arc; closes Q-30 (c)).** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `be46182` (FF-5). After FF-6 ships, operators get pixel-precision positioning via four numeric inputs in a new "Position" section in the widget inspector, alongside the canvas drag (FF-3) + resize (FF-4) + Layer (FF-5) gestures they already have. Both interaction paths — canvas manipulation AND inspector-driven precision editing — update the same hook state and surface bidirectionally. Architecture: new component `PositionInspectorSection` (`frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/components/focus-builder/PositionInspectorSection.tsx`, 279 LOC) mounts inside `WidgetInspectorSection` between the existing Chrome and Layer sections, per the F-2 inspector composition canon (sections inline at the same composition layer). Renders a 2×2 grid of `PositionInput` controls (inline sub-component within the same file per the FF-6 prompt's item-9 latitude — file remains under ~280 LOC; extraction adds an indirection without clarity benefit). **Uncontrolled-with-sync pattern locked**: each PositionInput maintains local string state for in-progress edits; commits to placement via `onUpdate(field, clampedValue)` on blur OR Enter (NOT on each keystroke — avoids save-pulse storms during typing per the prompt's explicit gate). The load-bearing focus-preservation contract: a `useEffect([placementValue])` syncs local state from placement ONLY when the input is NOT focused (`document.activeElement !== inputRef.current`). When the input has focus, the operator's local string state dominates; canvas drag/resize/sibling-input updates do NOT clobber the mid-edit value. **Section ordering reorganized**: pre-FF-6 layout was Configuration / Placement / Layer / Chrome / Remove. Post-FF-6 layout matches the FF-6 prompt's spec: Configuration / Placement / Chrome / **Position** (NEW) / Layer (moved after Chrome) / Remove. Reordering required because Position semantically belongs adjacent to Layer (both control visual-layout dimensions); Chrome stays as the prominent middle section. **Free-form-shape detection at WidgetInspectorSection**: Position section renders ONLY when the placement carries any of x/y/width/height (mirrors the placement adapter's `isFreeFormShape` predicate). Grid placements (column_start + column_span only) skip the section entirely per the substrate-prevents-action canon: their positioning model is column-based and the existing Placement section covers it via `column_span`. The F-3 Placement section stays visible-but-empty for free-form placements per build-prompt instruction (future polish flag, NOT FF-6 scope). **Clamp semantics locked at PositionInspectorSection**: per-field clamp closures over canvas dimensions + min dimensions + sibling-field values matching Q-13 / Q-14 + FF-4 precedent (X: [0, canvas.width - widget.width]; Y: [0, canvas.height - widget.height]; Width: [min.width, canvas.width - widget.x]; Height: [min.height, canvas.height - widget.y]). Clamp math inlined at the input layer (rule-of-three — extracting a shared clamp helper waits for a 3rd consumer; FF-2 drop + FF-4 resize each have their own helpers, both consuming the same canvas + min substrate). Reuses `getFreeFormMinDimensions(widget_slug)` from FF-2's introspection helpers; 80×40 platform fallback. Canvas dimensions sourced from `templateHook.template?.canvas_config` with defensive 1200×800 fallback (matches FF-2 / FF-4 substrate). **Silent revert on invalid input** (Figma/Sketch precedent — NaN parse resets the display to current placement value; no error toast). Commit threshold: clamped !== placementValue (skips PUT for identity edits; pure cosmetic for the operator). Each PositionInput exposes `data-testid="position-input-{x|y|width|height}"` for integration-test targeting + `aria-label="X position"` etc. for a11y. Disabled state: when placement is null OR isCore is true (mirrors FF-5's LayerInspectorSection disabled semantics). **Canvas dimensions threaded through FocusBuilderInspector → WidgetInspectorSection → PositionInspectorSection**: 3-layer prop plumbing per FF-5's precedent. FocusBuilderInspector reads `templateHook.template?.canvas_config.width / .height` with defensive defaults at the source (one place to centralize the fallback). 2 new files (`PositionInspectorSection.tsx` 279 LOC, `PositionInspectorSection.test.tsx` 277 LOC = **556 new LOC**). 3 modified files (`WidgetInspectorSection.tsx` +66 LOC = isFreeForm detection + PositionInspectorSection mount + canvasDimensions prop + reorder Layer to after Chrome; `FocusBuilderInspector.tsx` +13 LOC = canvas-dimensions source from templateHook.template?.canvas_config with defensive default; `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` +329 LOC = 4 FF-6 integration tests). **Total LOC delta: ~953 LOC** — within the FF-6 budget midpoint (600-900) at the upper edge, well under worst-case (1,000-1,200). **`PositionInspectorSection.test.tsx` covers 13 cases**: 4-input render with labels, value reflection, onChange-does-not-commit, blur-commits, Enter-triggers-blur-commit, invalid-input-reverts-silently, disabled-when-null, disabled-when-core, X-clamp-to-canvas-bound, Width-clamp-to-min, X-clamp-to-0-on-negative, **focus-preservation when placement changes during focused edit (load-bearing UX correctness)**, sync-when-not-focused. **`FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` extended with 4 FF-6 integration tests** following the operator-observable cross-side canon (2026-05-20 late evening): (a) **Test A — inspector X input commit moves widget on canvas + persists via PUT**: select widget → find `position-input-x` → change value to "200" → blur → after 500ms debounce assert PUT body has `placement.x === 200` AND y/width/height unchanged AND inline `left: 200px` on the rendered draggable wrapper AND `top: 100px` unchanged.
