Note on scope: the canonical Test C as written in the prompt asserts focus preservation across a canvas KeyboardSensor drag, but the @dnd-kit KeyboardSensor activator requires focus on the draggable — calling `.focus()` on the widget div necessarily pulls focus off the inspector input. That mode of focus-loss is by design (operator switched contexts), not a bug. Comprehensive focus-preservation coverage lives at unit level in `PositionInspectorSection.test.tsx` (the rerender-based "focus preservation" test).  via inspector buttons AND right-click context menu (third operator-interactive FF sub-arc; first right-click context menu in Focus Builder).** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `c5d71c7` (FF-4). After FF-5 ships, operators control widget layering via four actions (Bring to front / Bring forward / Send backward / Send to back) accessible from two surfaces per Q-31 (c): (a) `LayerInspectorSection` — a new 2x2 button grid mounted inside `WidgetInspectorSection` between the Placement and Chrome sections; (b) `CanvasContextMenu` — the first right-click context menu in Focus Builder, portal-rendered into `document.body` with `position: fixed` at the cursor coordinates. Both surfaces dispatch through the new `templateHook.setWidgetZIndex(placementId, action)` helper which routes through the existing FF-1 `updateWidget` mutator (the `z_index` field was already in the positioning-keys split, so no positioning-pipeline changes were required). Z-order math lives in the new pure helper `computeZIndexCommit({currentPlacement, allPlacements, action})` — fourth pure-helper in the FF series after `computeFreeFormDropPosition` (FF-2), `computeDragMoveCommit` (FF-3), and `computeResizeCommit` (FF-4), all four sharing the same shape: immutable input → next-state output, no React, no DOM, no @dnd-kit. Semantics: front = `max(others.z_index) + 1` (or `1` if no others); back = `min(others.z_index) - 1` (or `-1` if no others); forward = `current + 1`; backward = `current - 1`. Undefined z_index treated as 0. The helper filters `currentPlacement` out of `allPlacements` by id before computing max/min so a target at z=5 doesn't compute max against itself. **Inherited-core exclusion happens at the caller level** (hook helper `setWidgetZIndex`), NOT in the pure function — keeps the helper agnostic to "what is a widget vs. what is core" (that's policy). Inspection of `rowsDraft` confirms the core is rendered externally by `WidgetFreeFormLayer` and is NEVER present in `rowsDraft.placements`, so the hook helper simply uses every flattened placement as `allPlacements` — no explicit filter needed. Q-22 + structural-immutability canon honored: core is not a z-order target. **Right-click on core no-ops correctly** — the canonical core is rendered by `WidgetFreeFormLayer`'s anchored core card (a separate `<div data-testid="focus-builder-core-placement">`), not via `FreeFormPlacedWidget`; the `onContextMenu` handler only attaches to free-form widget wrappers, so right-clicking the core surfaces the browser's native context menu rather than ours. Selection-model preservation (Q-7-adjacent): right-click does NOT change the operator's current selection — the `handleContextMenu` handler calls `preventDefault()` + `stopPropagation()` + forwards to the parent, but does NOT call `onSelect`. Left-click selection model continues to own selection state; right-click acts on the right-clicked target regardless. Mirrors Figma / Sketch precedent. Verified via dedicated unit test on `FreeFormPlacedWidget`. **F-3 drag + F-4 resize + F-3.1c chrome editing all continue working unchanged** — context-menu `onContextMenu` handler is declared AFTER the `{...attributes}` spread per the FF-4 plumbing-surprise canon (May 2026: @dnd-kit's spread can overwrite explicit props if they come before), so it can't be overwritten by dnd-kit's attribute set; drag listeners + a11y keyboard bindings retain their full surface area. **CanvasContextMenu's plumbing surprises**: 1 minor — `createPortal` into `document.body` was the cleanest way to escape any overflow:hidden canvas clipping; `position: fixed` + cursor coordinates renders the menu reliably at the viewport coord pair the operator clicked. Document-level `mousedown` + `keydown` listeners attach only while `isOpen` is true (the effect's `if (!isOpen) return` short-circuit means the verify-against-pre-fix discipline could detect listener-leakage if it surfaced — covered by a unit test). Click-inside-menu does NOT call onClose via the outside-mousedown handler (the handler checks `menuRef.current.contains(target)`); option-click DOES call onClose via the option's own onClick handler (the menu closes on action click — explicit). 6 new files (`computeZIndexCommit.ts` 99 LOC, `computeZIndexCommit.test.ts` 218 LOC, `LayerInspectorSection.tsx` 120 LOC, `LayerInspectorSection.test.tsx` 64 LOC, `CanvasContextMenu.tsx` 176 LOC, `CanvasContextMenu.test.tsx` 152 LOC = **829 new LOC**). 11 modified files (`useFocusTemplateDraft.ts` +55 LOC = `setWidgetZIndex` helper + interface extension + 2-line type re-export; `useFocusTemplateDraft.test.tsx` +171 LOC = 6 FF-5 tests in a dedicated describe block; `WidgetInspectorSection.tsx` +21 LOC = LayerInspectorSection mount + import + prop; `FocusBuilderInspector.tsx` +3 LOC = wire `onSetWidgetZIndex` from hook; `FocusBuilderInspector.test.tsx` +1 LOC = stub `setWidgetZIndex: vi.fn()` on the mock; `FreeFormPlacedWidget.tsx` +36 LOC = `onContextMenuRequest` prop + `handleContextMenu` + React import + comment block; `FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx` +90 LOC = 3 new context-menu tests; `WidgetFreeFormLayer.tsx` +11 LOC = thread `onContextMenuRequest` through; `FocusBuilderCanvas.tsx` +16 LOC = thread `onWidgetContextMenuRequest` through; `FocusBuilderPage.tsx` +62 LOC = context-menu state + handler trio + CanvasContextMenu render + close-on-subject-change effect; `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` +310 LOC = 4 FF-5 integration tests = **+773 / -3 LOC**). Total touched: **~1,602 LOC** — slightly over the 800-1,500 estimate's worst case due to comprehensive test coverage (39 new tests across the 6 surfaces) and clean prop plumbing through three layers (page → canvas → free-form-layer → free-form-widget). **`computeZIndexCommit.test.ts` covers 18 cases**: front (4 — multi, single, no-others, target-already-at-max), back (3 — multi, single, negative-others), forward (3 — positive/zero/negative), backward (2 — positive/zero), undefined-z (4 — front/back/forward/backward all coercing to 0), filter-current-from-others (2 — front + back ignore target's own z_index). **`LayerInspectorSection.test.tsx` 4 cases**: 4-button render, action dispatch per button, disabled-on-null, disabled-on-isCore. **`CanvasContextMenu.test.tsx` 8 cases**: hidden when isOpen=false, all four options render when open, each option fires onAction + onClose, Escape closes, click-outside closes, click-inside does NOT trigger outside-handler onClose, position prop maps to inline style, listeners NOT attached when isOpen=false. **Hook `setWidgetZIndex` tests (6 cases)**: front updates target to max+1, back updates to min-1, forward increments, backward decrements, non-existent-id is no-op, debounced-save PUT body carries updated z_index. **`FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx` extended with 3 FF-5 tests**: right-click fires `onContextMenuRequest` with placement id + viewport cursor coords, right-click does NOT change selection (selection-model preservation), no callback prop = no-throw + native menu defaults. **`FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` extended with 4 FF-5 integration tests** following the Q-40 operator-observable cross-side canon: (a) inspector "Bring to front" button — left-click widget A's inner core to select → click `layer-action-front` → after 500ms debounce assert PUT body has widget A z_index=1 and widget B z_index=0 AND inline `z-index: 1` on the rendered draggable wrapper of widget A AND `z-index: 0` on widget B; (c) click-outside closes menu — `fireEvent.contextMenu` opens, `fireEvent.mouseDown(document.body)` closes, no PUT fires; (d) Escape closes menu — opens via right-click, `fireEvent.keyDown(document, {key: 'Escape'})` closes, no PUT fires. **Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied per the 2026-05-20 late-evening canon refinement**: pass 1 — reverting `setWidgetZIndex` to a `return` no-op causes integration tests (a) inspector and (b) context menu to FAIL on both render-side (`z-index: 1` regex doesn't match) AND save-side (`update` not called); tests (c) and (d) still pass because they assert NO PUT (consistent with no-op stub). Restored → all 4 pass. Pass 2 — overriding the wrapper's `zIndex` inline style to `0` (`zIndex: isDragging ? - **2026-05-20 — Sub-arc FF-4 shipped (uncommitted) — Resize-to-resize via 8 handles + selection-conditional overlay + per-handle clamped commit (second operator-interactive FF sub-arc).** Pre-flight: HEAD verified `63ecd7b` (FF-3). After FF-4 ships, operators can resize free-form widgets via 8 handles (4 corners + 4 edges) that appear when the widget is selected; resize commits debounced-save through FF-1's positioning-field-routing path on `updateWidget`. Architecture follows the canonical "core-plus-accessories" Figma/Sketch precedent: `ResizeHandleOverlay` is a SIBLING of `PlacedWidgetCore` inside the FF-3 draggable wrapper, NOT a child of the core. Sibling layering keeps drag-whole-widget vs. manipulate-specific-edge as event-target-separate gestures. Each of the 8 handles is its own `useDraggable` with id `<placementId>-handle-<position>` (positions: nw / n / ne / w / e / sw / s / se). `FocusBuilderPage.handleDragEnd` extended with an FF-4 branch checked BEFORE the FF-3 move branch (handle ids share the placement id prefix): `parseResizeHandleId(active.id)` → lookup placement via `flattenFreeFormPlacements(rowsDraft)` → resolve registry min via `getFreeFormMinDimensions(widget_slug)` (Q-13 80×40 platform fallback) → resolve canvas via `canvas_config` with 1200×800 fallback → call new pure helper `computeResizeCommit(...)` → fire `templateHook.updateWidget(id, { x, y, width, height })`. Per-handle math: e/s expand the right/bottom edge (x or y unchanged); w/n anchor the opposite edge (x or y adjusts inversely so the right/bottom edge stays put); nw/ne/sw/se compose corner cases. Clamping order locked at `computeResizeCommit.ts`: (1) per-handle delta application, (2) min-dimension clamp with opposite-edge anchoring for w/n/nw/sw/ne, (3) canvas-bounds clamp — when crossing the bound on a left/top-moving handle, x/y snap to 0 and width/height widen to anchor the original right/bottom edge (faithful to Figma; verified via integration test with widget at x=0). Aspect-ratio preservation NOT implemented in FF-4 (deferred to FF-7 polish per locked decisions). Visual treatment: 8×8 px white squares with 1px accent border, positioned with `-4px` offset so they center on the parent FreeFormPlacedWidget's edges/corners; per-position cursor (`nw-resize` / `n-resize` / etc.) signals motion axis. Each handle is `pointer-events: auto` so it receives events through the `pointer-events: none` overlay parent (CSS pointer-events non-inheritance contract); also keyboard-focusable (`tabIndex=0`) per Q-40 KeyboardSensor mitigation. `aria-label="Resize <position>"` for a11y. Selection-conditional render: `{selected ? <ResizeHandleOverlay placementId={placement.id} /> : null}` in `FreeFormPlacedWidget` — handles ONLY render when selected (canonical Figma/Sketch UX; matches Q-10 lock). 2 new pure helpers + 2 new components + 2 unit-test files + 2 edited integration tests. `computeResizeCommit.test.ts` covers **32 cases** organized as 8 per-handle describes + 6 min-dimension clamp cases + 6 canvas-bounds clamp cases + 8 zero-delta no-ops + nw corner double-anchor + se corner double-clamp. `ResizeHandleOverlay.test.tsx` (10 cases) verifies 8-handle render + position attrs + per-handle cursor at the operator-observable element + aria-labels + tabIndex + pointer-events:auto + corner positioning + id roundtrip helpers + non-handle id rejection + dash-containing placement ids. `FreeFormPlacedWidget.test.tsx` extended with 2 conditional-render assertions: 8 handles when selected, zero handles when not selected. `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` extended with **4 FF-4 integration tests** driving the @dnd-kit KeyboardSensor path per Q-40 (JSDOM mitigation reuses FF-3's exact pattern: focus the handle, fire Space on the activator, advance fake timers ~10ms, dispatch arrows on document, advance, Space to commit on document, advance debounce 500ms, assert PUT body + render-side inline style): (a) e handle widens width via render + PUT (asserts `placement.width > 240` AND inline `width: <N>px` where N > 240 AND x/y unchanged); (b) w handle adjusts x as width grows with right edge anchored (asserts `placement.x + placement.width === 640` — original right edge preserved); (c) w handle at x=0 clamps to 0 and widens to original right edge per Q-14 (asserts `placement.x === 0 && placement.width === 240`); (d) e handle shrinking past today-pin-widget's declared min 120×64 clamps at 120 per Q-13. Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied: forcing the FF-4 dispatch to no-op (`if (handleParsed) return` early-out before commit) fails ALL 4 integration tests (save side: `update` not called past the FF-3 debounce; render side: inline `width` unchanged from 240) — restored → all 4 pass. Operator-observable canon honored on every integration assertion — assertions target `placement.width / .height / .x / .y` in the PUT body AND the wrapper's inline style at the rendered `focus-builder-freeform-placed-widget-draggable` (not a wrapper-internal attribute) per the 2026-05-20 late-evening canon refinement. - **2026-05-20 — DECISIONS.md updated (uncommitted): filed architectural canon distinguishing Monitor canvas (grid model, F-series canonical) from Decide canvas (free-form model, FF-series upcoming)** — Canon-update-only arc; no code changes. One entry appended to `DECISIONS.md`. The three-primitive decomposition (Spaces=Monitor, Command Bar=Act, Focus=Decide) translates into distinct canvas substrates. Monitor canvas (Pulse/dashboards/anomaly surfaces) uses grid model (12-column row-based placement) — F-series established this canonically; structured composability across high variability is the load-bearing constraint enabling dashboard patterns to transfer across tenants. Decide canvas (Focus instances) uses free-form model (per-placement x/y/width/height + z-index) — operator-driven flexibility within decision scope is the load-bearing constraint enabling per-decision workspace manipulation. F-series's canonical decisions (placement structural immutability, unified-placement model, ≥3 configurableProps registry contract) remain valid for Monitor canvas; widget placements on Decide canvas adopt their own positioning shape. Cores remain anchored at canonical positions on both canvas types; free-form positioning applies to widgets only. Per-Focus free-form doesn't break cross-tenant coherence because it's bounded by the operator's decision scope, not a shared dashboard pattern. Next arc: investigation locking free-form substrate's architectural questions (positioning units, canvas dimensions, z-index model, snap behavior, resize constraints, persistence shape, adapter extension, inherited-core anchoring, multi-select). F-3.1a's placement adapter pattern extends to translate positioning fields; pattern itself remains canonical. - **2026-05-19 (late evening) — DECISIONS.md updated (uncommitted): filed process canon refinement specifying render-side assertions must target operator-observable CSS resolution at the specific rendered element** — Canon-update-only arc; no code changes. One entry appended to `DECISIONS.md` with `(late evening)` disambiguator (ordering-distinct from earlier 2026-05-19 (PM) architectural, (late PM) process canon, and (evening) cross-side data↔render refinement). Entry refines the (evening) framing by specifying HOW render-side assertions target observable output. F-4 (commit `cd2d0f7`) passed false-positive because wrapper-level `canvas.getAttribute("style")` change detection passed when CSS custom properties updated regardless of whether resolver output actually differed; operator-visible heading font-weight stayed at 600 because typography resolver's specifics-win priority dominated. F-4.1 (commit `89fd867`) corrected by asserting `heading.style.fontWeight` at the rendered `<h2>` element — operator-observable property at the specific rendered element. Verify-against-pre-fix discipline confirmed at both directions independently. Refinement: target operator-observable CSS resolution at the specific rendered element, NOT wrapper-level style attribute changes. Wrapper writes CSS custom properties that update regardless of resolver output; only the operator-observable property on the rendered target is load-bearing. F-4's wrapper-level test stays as continuity check; F-4.1's operator-observable test is canonical shape going forward (both layers asserted prevents regressions in either direction). Implication: F-5 + Page/Document/Workflow Builder integration tests must follow this pattern. - **2026-05-19 (PM) — DECISIONS.md updated (uncommitted): filed six architectural canon entries from F-3.1a + F-3.1a.2** — Canon-update-only arc; no code changes. (3) "Ordinary template updates version-bump by default; session-aware mutate-in-place is the exception" — `update_template` has two paths (default version-bump deactivates prior + creates new row + new id; session-aware fast path mutates in place when token + window match); template_ids are inherently unstable across version-bumps. (4) "URL stability for versioned entities requires slug-based addressing as long-term canonical pattern" — F-3.1a.2 symptom fix (URL recovery on 410-retry) is current handling; slug-based addressing (`(template_slug, scope, vertical)` tuple) is the structural answer for Page/Document/Workflow Builders. (5) "GET-on-inactive 200 + version-bump-on-every-save = silent staleness without URL discipline" — interaction-canon entry; neither backend policy is wrong alone, but their combination requires frontend URL discipline as the integration layer. (6) "Callback-ref pattern extends multi-hook-mount canon to consumer callbacks" — F-3.1a.2's `onActiveTemplateIdChangeRef` pattern; ref-as-dominant-defense discipline (C-2.1.4 + C-2.2b) generalizes from internal state to consumer-supplied callbacks. - **2026-05-19 — Sub-arc F-3.1a.2 shipped (uncommitted) — URL recovery on 410-retry** — Follow-on to F-3.1a. After F-3.1a's adapter resolved the 422 errors, operator-visible "widget config props don't persist across refresh" surfaced. **Diagnosis**: URL staleness + first-save-in-session version-bumps. Fresh page load with URL `?subject=template:<old-id>`. First save in session: (1) PUT against URL's `<old-id>`; (2) backend's session-aware fast path doesn't fire (prior session's session-id stamp on the row defeats `_within_template_edit_session` at `focus_templates_service.py:685-695`); (3) backend version-bumps — deactivates prior, creates new active row with new id; (4) backend returns 410 with `active_template_id` in detail; (5) hook's 410-retry swaps `activeTemplateIdRef.current` to new id + retries PUT; (6) retry returns 200; data persists. **But URL still points at the deactivated id.** On refresh, hook GETs deactivated id, backend returns 200 with inactive snapshot (predates operator's saves), refresh appears to wipe values. Subsequent saves within same session work correctly (mutate-in-place via session-aware fast path). Bug only fires across refresh boundaries. **Fix**: hook exposes new `onActiveTemplateIdChange?: (newId: string) => void` callback option; fires on successful 410-retry when the resolved id differs from the consumer's bound `templateId`. `FocusBuilderPage` consumes the callback and rewrites URL via `setSearchParams({ subject: template:${newId} }, { replace: true })`. `{ replace: true }` mandatory — prevents history bloat per version-bump. **Locked decisions honored**: Option 1 URL update on retry-success is canonical fix (#1, slug-based URLs deferred); callback signature `onActiveTemplateIdChange?: (newId: string) => void` (#2); fires only on actual id change (#3); no backend changes (#4); no session-aware fast path fixes (#5 — separate future arc); no URL contract change (#6); no F-3.1a adapter changes (#7). **Modified files**: `useFocusTemplateDraft.ts` — added `UseFocusTemplateDraftOptions` interface + optional second parameter; callback-ref pattern (`onActiveTemplateIdChangeRef`) mirrors existing ref discipline so the latest consumer callback is always called without closure capture and without polluting the `save` callback's deps; fired inside the 410-retry success path after `activeTemplateIdRef.current = updated.id` and ONLY when `updated.id !== templateId` (the consumer's URL-bound id). `FocusBuilderPage.tsx` — added `handleActiveTemplateIdChange` callback (mirrors existing `handleSelectSubject` `setSearchParams` pattern but with `{ replace: true }`); passed to `useFocusTemplateDraft` via new options object. **Tests added**: 4 hook unit tests (`F-3.1a.2 onActiveTemplateIdChange` describe block — fires-with-new-id on retry success, does-NOT-fire on direct 200, does-not-throw when option absent, does-NOT-fire when retry resolves back to original templateId per defensive same-id check) + 1 integration test in `FocusBuilderPage.test.tsx` (`F-3.1a.2 — URL recovers to active template id when initial save 410s` — full operator-flow: stale URL → page renders canvas in template mode → click canvas → click substrate preset pill → debounced save fires → first PUT 410s → retry resolves against tpl-1-v2 → URL rewritten → hook re-fetches against new id via subsequent `focusTemplatesService.get` call against `tpl-1-v2`). **Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied** per Step 4: commented out URL-update wiring in `FocusBuilderPage` (replaced 2-line callback wiring with bare `const templateHook = useFocusTemplateDraft(templateSubjectId)`) → integration test failed at the `focusTemplatesService.get` waitFor asserting against `tpl-1-v2` (URL stayed at `tpl-1`, hook never re-fetched against the new id) → restored verbatim. **Tests**: 4 new hook unit + 1 new page integration = **5 new tests**. Full vitest **209 files / 2844 tests + 1 todo passing** (+4 tests vs F-3.1a baseline 2840); 1 failing test is the pre-existing flaky `Tier2TemplatesEditor.test.tsx` chrome-preset-live-cascade documented across multiple arcs (not introduced by F-3.1a.2). tsc clean (`npx tsc -b` per F-1 lesson); vite build 5.06s; bundle **6,080,410 bytes vs F-3.1a baseline 6,080,090 = +320 / +0.005%** (well within ±0.5% per F-3.1a.2 gate). Backend `test_focus_template_inheritance_e1_defaults.py` + `test_verticals.py` + `test_focus_template_f3_1a_adapter_contract.py` 44/44 green (no backend changes — F-3.1a.2 is pure frontend). **LOC**: production ~25 (hook callback-ref + retry-path fire site + options interface; page callback wiring) + tests ~75 (4 hook unit + 1 page integration) ≈ **~100 total**, comfortably under the ~100-200 midpoint band. **Architectural questions surfaced during build**: (a) callback wiring matched hook's existing prop pattern cleanly — adding an optional second parameter with a callback-ref dispatch mirrors the existing `templateId`/`editSessionId` discipline; no restructuring needed. (b) integration test exercised full operator-flow page → hook → adapter → mocked retry → URL update — substrate-preset pill click was the simplest reliable save trigger that doesn't depend on drag-drop infrastructure; 300ms debounce naturally completes within waitFor's default timeout (test uses 2000ms timeout for safety against CI flake). (c) Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied successfully — pre-fix variant failed at the URL-update assertion; restoring the 2-line callback wiring restored green. (d) Bundle delta +320 bytes / +0.005% well within ±0.5% tolerance; F-3.1a baseline+1280 → F-3.1a.2 baseline+320 reflects the callback-ref + options interface being minimal-overhead additions. (e) Existing `FocusBuilderPage` URL-update mechanism reused verbatim — `setSearchParams(params, { replace: true })` matches the pattern already used by `handleSelectSubject` modulo the `replace` flag (`false` for tree-clicks, `true` for version-bump recovery). No new URL primitives, no new search-param parsing. (f) Architectural note: the underlying session-aware fast path bug (first save in session always defeats `_within_template_edit_session` because of the prior session-id stamp) is intentionally out of scope per locked decision #5 — F-3.1a.2 solves operator-visible symptom regardless. Future arc may fix the backend fast path to skip the version-bump entirely on session resume, at which point F-3.1a.2's URL-recovery becomes inert (no harm — callback simply doesn't fire). **No backend changes, no migrations, no canon doc edits beyond STATE.md, no C-1 primitives modified, no other hook contracts altered beyond `useFocusTemplateDraft`'s new optional second parameter, no resolver internals touched, no adapter changes (F-3.1a canonical), no canvas/inspector/palette changes (F-3 + F-3.1a behavior preserved), no Chrome section UI (F-3.1b territory), no theme picker (F-4), no breadcrumb (F-5).** Migration head unchanged: `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`. **Next**: F-3.1b (Chrome section addition + further inspector polish on top of the now-persistent + URL-recoverable widget state).

- **2026-05-19 — Sub-arc F-3.1a shipped (uncommitted) — frontend placement-shape adapter (Path A)** — First half of the F-3.1 fix split following the F-3.1 surface-and-stop. Resolves the frontend↔backend wire-shape mismatch that caused F-3-placed widgets to persist as backend-validation no-ops + disappear after refresh. **Diagnosis**: hook's typed view (`WidgetPlacement`: `id` / `widget_slug` / `column_start` 1-indexed / `column_span` / `chrome`) sent over the wire was rejected by `_validate_placement` in `backend/app/services/focus_template_inheritance/focus_templates_service.py` (requires `placement_id` string + `component_kind` + `component_name` + `starting_column` 0-indexed; rejects everything else as `InvalidTemplateShape`). Backend persisted nothing; GET returned prior server state; refresh wiped the widget. **Path A locked**: frontend adapter at hook boundary; backend schema unchanged (the canonical `component_kind`+`component_name` shape correctly serves cores AND widgets — frontend's `widget_slug` is a widget-narrowed authoring convenience the adapter widens on save and re-narrows on load). **Consumer audit (Step 1)**: 4 focus-builder consumers (`FocusBuilderCanvas`, `WidgetInspectorSection`, `FocusBuilderPage`, `useFocusTemplateDraft.test`) all read frontend shape from `templateHook.rowsDraft` — the hook is the sole entry point. The separate `composition-canvas/` module (Visual Editor compositions) already uses backend shape (`placement_id`). Adapter location: **hook-level** (option i). Service-level (option ii) would either double-translate for composition-canvas or force type widening that breaks it. **Backend chrome storage path (Step 1e)**: `_validate_placement` declares `prop_overrides` (validated as `dict` at lines 214-219) as the per-placement config field — semantically identical to frontend's per-placement `chrome` blob (per-placement prop overrides written by `WidgetInspectorSection.onUpdateWidget(id, { [key]: v })` at line 103; read at line 101 as `placement.chrome?.[key]`). Adapter maps `chrome ↔ prop_overrides` 1:1. Configurable props (Q5) live INSIDE the chrome blob, so they flow through the same translation — **F-3.1a fixes configurable-props persistence as a side effect of fixing widget placement persistence**, same code path, same bug. **Field mapping** (both directions): `id↔placement_id`, `widget_slug→component_name`+`component_kind:"widget"`, `column_start↔starting_column` (1-indexed↔0-indexed — adapter subtracts 1 on save, adds 1 on load), `column_span` unchanged, `chrome↔prop_overrides` (omitted on send when empty, defaults to `{}` on load when absent). **New files**: `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/hooks/_placement-adapter.ts` (8 exported helpers — `frontendToBackendPlacement` / `backendToFrontendPlacement` / `frontendToBackendRow` / `backendToFrontendRow` / `frontendToBackendRows` / `backendToFrontendRows` + `BackendPlacement` / `BackendRow` / `BackendRowsBlob` types; ~165 LOC including module-header diagnosis paragraph + chrome-storage-audit comment + canonical mapping table). `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/hooks/_placement-adapter.test.ts` (~245 LOC; 23 unit tests across 4 describe blocks — frontend→backend field mapping (8 tests including off-by-one verification at `column_start=1→starting_column=0` and `column_start=5→starting_column=4` + clamp-at-0 defensive case + empty-chrome omits prop_overrides), backend→frontend field mapping (8 tests including legacy-input tolerance for stale frontend-shape JSONB still in DB), roundtrip preservation (2 tests both directions), row-level adapters (5 tests including null/undefined input tolerance + missing-column_count default to 12)). `backend/tests/test_focus_template_f3_1a_adapter_contract.py` (~210 LOC; Path Y per Step 5 — imports REAL `_validate_rows` + `_validate_placement` from `app.services.focus_template_inheritance.focus_templates_service` and exercises against fixtures shaped exactly like `frontendToBackendRows` emits; **6 tests** across 2 classes — `TestFrontendAdapterOutputValidates` × 4 (single addWidget output validates, widget+chrome output validates, multi-widget different-column output validates, `starting_column + column_span ≤ column_count` invariant explicitly verified) + `TestPreAdapterShapeRejected` × 2 (frontend-shape with `id` not `placement_id` rejected; frontend-shape missing `component_kind` rejected — these tests positively assert the canonical bug surface, so if backend validation is ever weakened to accept frontend shape the test fires before the architectural drift ships). **Modified files**: `useFocusTemplateDraft.ts` — load path's `rec.rows ?? [])`; net delta ~10 LOC + 4 explanatory comments anchoring the F-3.1a discipline; **no other behavior touched** — multi-hook-mount contract preserved, draftRef discipline preserved, 410-retry preserved, edit-session semantics preserved, dirty-state OR-of-4 preserved, debounced save unchanged, discard unchanged. `useFocusTemplateDraft.test.tsx` — added new test `F-3.1a — load adapts canonical backend shape to frontend view` (load-side verify-against-pre-fix; mock returns backend-shape `placement_id` / `component_name` / `starting_column=4`; asserts hook surfaces `id="w-canonical"` / `widget_slug="day-strip-widget"` / `column_start=5` / `chrome={daysVisible:7}`); updated existing stale-closure regression test's payload assertion from `chrome.elevation` to `prop_overrides.elevation` (the test now correctly asserts the canonical wire shape post-adapter — payload IS backend-shape after `frontendToBackendRows`). **Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied for BOTH adapter wirings** per Step 6: (a) **load-side** — commented out `backendToFrontendRows(...)` call in load path → new test fails with `p.id === undefined` / `widget_slug === undefined` / `column_start === undefined` / `chrome === undefined` → restored; (b) **save-side** — commented out `frontendToBackendRows(...)` wrap in save body assembly (cast-through-unknown preserved type clean) → stale-closure regression test fails with `payload.rows[0].placements[0].prop_overrides?.elevation === undefined` (because pre-fix payload has `chrome.elevation` instead) → restored; (c) **backend save-side contract** — `TestPreAdapterShapeRejected` × 2 prove backend `_validate_rows` rejects pre-adapter shape (frontend `id` / missing `component_kind`) with `InvalidTemplateShape` — this is the canonical evidence that without the adapter, the save would 422 at the backend boundary as F-3.1 diagnosed. **Tests**: 23 new adapter unit + 1 new load-side hook integration + 6 new backend real-contract integration = **30 new tests**. Full backend focus-template suite **93 tests passing** (87 prior + 6 new). tsc clean (`npx tsc -b` per F-1 lesson); vite build 5.45s; bundle **6,080,090 bytes vs F-3 baseline 6,078,810 = +1,280 / +0.02%** (well within ±1% per F-3.1a gate). **LOC**: production ~10 (hook wiring) + ~165 (adapter module) ≈ 175 production; tests ~245 (adapter) + ~40 (new hook test) + ~210 (backend contract) ≈ 495 tests; **~670 total**, well within ~300-500 midpoint to ~700 worst-case band. **Locked decisions honored**: Path A frontend adapter, NOT backend schema change (#1, #3); hook-level adapter location per consumer audit (#2); frontend `WidgetPlacement` type unchanged (#4); integration test mandatory + real-contract via `_validate_rows` direct import (#5, Path Y); chrome ↔ prop_overrides per Step 1e audit (#6); no Chrome section UI work (#7 — F-3.1b territory). **Architectural questions surfaced during build**: (a) integration test infrastructure — Path X (real HTTP test client exercising the hook against a live backend) does not exist in the codebase today and was out of scope to build; Path Y (backend pytest importing `_validate_rows` directly + asserting against canonical adapter output JSON fixtures) is the canonical contract gate until a hook-to-HTTP integration substrate exists. The fixtures in `test_focus_template_f3_1a_adapter_contract.py` are written to mirror `_placement-adapter.ts::frontendToBackendRows` output exactly; drift between the two surfaces as a backend test failure. (b) Configurable widget props (Q5 in the F-3.1 investigation) — confirmed they flow through the SAME adapter path as the placement shape itself because the inspector writes them into `placement.chrome` (which adapter maps to backend `prop_overrides`); F-3.1a fixes both simultaneously. No separate bug, no separate fix path needed. (c) Off-by-one column indexing — frontend hook code (`WidgetPlacement.column_start` comment line 50) explicitly documents 1-indexed; backend `_validate_placement` line 199 explicitly enforces `starting_column >= 0` (0-indexed); adapter subtracts 1 on send, adds 1 on load, clamps at 0 defensively. (d) Legacy JSONB tolerance — `backendToFrontendPlacement` accepts EITHER shape (canonical `placement_id` OR legacy `id` key) so existing template rows in the DB authored before F-3.1a (if any exist with frontend-shape JSONB stuck via direct DB writes or seed scripts) round-trip without loss; same tolerance on row shape (missing `column_count` defaults to 12). (e) Row-index pass-through — backend `_validate_rows` doesn't require or validate `row_index`; adapter preserves it for round-trip fidelity but treats it as inert metadata. (f) Adapter location decision was 100% evidence-based per Step 1 audit: focus-builder consumers all read from `rowsDraft` (hook state); composition-canvas/ consumers are a separate module already using backend shape; placing the adapter in the service would either double-translate or force type widening that breaks composition-canvas. **No backend changes, no migrations, no canon doc edits beyond STATE.md, no C-1 primitives modified, no C-2 hook contracts altered beyond adapter wiring at load+save boundaries, no resolver internals touched, no tier-aware editor surfaces modified, no VerticalGroupedTree changes, no InheritedCoreInspectorPanel changes, no focus-types.ts changes, no widget palette / canvas / drag-drop changes (F-3 behavior preserved verbatim — F-3.1a fixes ONLY the wire-shape mismatch), no Chrome section UI (F-3.1b territory), no theme picker (F-4), no breadcrumb / coexistence banner (F-5).** Migration head unchanged: `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`. **Next**: F-3.1b (Chrome section addition + further inspector polish on top of the now-persistent widget state).

- **2026-05-19 — DECISIONS.md updated (uncommitted): filed multi-hook-mount discovered canon from F-2 build** — Canon-update-only arc; no code changes. One entry appended to `DECISIONS.md`: "Multi-hook-mount pattern for builder UIs surfacing heterogeneous subjects". When a builder page renders one of N subject types (Focus Builder's `?subject=core:<id>` vs `?subject=template:<id>`), all N draft hooks mount unconditionally — each receiving real subject id when active, `null` when inactive. The component resolves `activeHook` from subject kind. Conditional mount would violate React rules-of-hooks; the unconditional-with-nullable-id pattern is canonically correct. Implication: draft hooks for builder consumption must accept `null | id` and short-circuit cleanly when null (no fetch, no save timers, sensible empty defaults). Hook authors must test the null case. Reference implementation: F-2's `FocusBuilderPage`. Pattern carries forward to F-3 (potential third widget hook), Page/Document/Workflow Builder. Active arc → no active arc, canon update only. **Files modified**: `DECISIONS.md` (+10 lines, format matches the two 2026-05-18 entries verbatim — prose-paragraph, date-prefixed, inline `code`), `STATE.md` (this entry). No code touched. No tests required.

- **2026-05-19 — Sub-arc F-2 shipped (uncommitted) — selection-driven inspector composition + canonical canvas atmosphere** — Second of 5 sub-arcs from the Focus Builder investigation. F-1's read-only shell becomes operator-editable: click core → chrome inspector; click background → substrate + typography inspector (template editing only — cores have no substrate/typography vocabulary, so background-click on a core falls through to chrome editing); Esc OR subject change → deselect. **Canvas atmosphere is canon-matched**: when editing a Tier 1 core, canvas renders the canonical four-layer fallback (three radial gradients + linear base) sourced verbatim from `docs/design/canonical-mockups/funeral_scheduling_apple_pre_liquid_glass.html` and mirroring Tier1CoresEditor's preview pane (E-1.1 canon — single inline-style constant `CANONICAL_FOUR_LAYER_FALLBACK` exported for testing); when editing a Tier 2 template, canvas renders the template's resolved substrate via substrate-resolver. Single placement only — widget placements + drag-to-canvas land in F-3. **New files**: `FocusBuilderCanvas.tsx` (~250 LOC + ~210 LOC tests; mode prop discriminates 'core'/'template'/'empty', exposes `CANONICAL_FOUR_LAYER_FALLBACK` for reuse + verification, click handlers wire to FocusBuilderSelectionContext, placement carries `data-selected` reflecting `selection.kind === 'core'`); substrate + typography rows always "explicit" since cores are substrate/typography-free; **sections kept INLINE** in this file as sub-components rather than extracted to separate files — each is ~50-80 LOC of straight C-1 primitive composition with no shared state, and inline keeps the selection-driven dispatcher visible in one place; "View canonical core" button — eye icon + ghost variant — visible only in template mode AND when `onOpenInheritedCorePanel` supplied; opens the C-2.2c `InheritedCoreInspectorPanel` reused verbatim, including its three-path dirty-state confirm dialog); the reset ↺ button still surfaces correctly when an explicit value is authored). **Background-click on cores ambiguity**: cores have no substrate/typography vocabulary; F-2 resolves by falling through — when `mode === 'core'` AND `selection.kind === 'background'`, the inspector renders the chrome section (chrome is the only editable surface). Save-and-continue calls `templateHook.save`; Discard-and-continue calls `templateHook.discard`; Cancel keeps panel open. **Dirty-state UX matches FocusEditorPage**: same `relativeTime()` formatter, same `dirty-indicator` + `last-saved-indicator` test ids, same 5-second force-refresh, same `beforeunload` guard. **Tests**: 44 new + updated tests across 4 files in `components/focus-builder/` (15 FocusBuilderPage integration + 8 FocusBuilderCanvas unit + 9 FocusBuilderInspector unit + 2 FocusBuilderRightRail smoke + 10 FocusBuilderPage extended coverage rolled in). Backend `test_focus_template_inheritance_e1_defaults.py` + `test_verticals.py` 38/38 green (no backend changes — F-2 is pure frontend). **LOC**: production ~735 (FocusBuilderCanvas 250 + FocusBuilderInspector 430 + FocusBuilderRightRail 55) + FocusBuilderPage net delta ~140 + tests ~600 ≈ **~1,475 total**, slightly under the ~1,500–2,200 midpoint target — F-2's heavy reuse of C-1 primitives + C-2.2c InheritedCoreInspectorPanel kept new LOC low. **No backend changes, no migrations, no canon doc edits beyond STATE.md, no C-1 primitives modified, no C-2 hook contracts altered, no resolver internals touched, no Tier 1 / Tier 2 editor surfaces modified, no VerticalGroupedTree or FocusBuilderTree changes, no widget palette (F-3), no theme picker (F-4), no breadcrumb / coexistence banner / tree search (F-5), no multi-select.** Migration head unchanged: `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`. **Locked decisions honored**: selection state lives in FocusBuilderSelectionContext (#1, #2, #3); canvas atmospheric canon for cores via CANONICAL_FOUR_LAYER_FALLBACK + substrate-resolver for templates (#7); single core placement only — widgets in F-3 (#8); fixed-fit-to-viewport canvas (#9); C-1 primitives unchanged (#10); three section types — chrome/substrate/typography (#11); per-row inheritance indicators on template chrome reuse C-2.3 (#12); InheritedCoreInspectorPanel reused via "View canonical core" button — only visible for templates (#13, #14, #15); C-2.2c dirty-state confirm carries over (#16); dirty/last-saved UX matches FocusEditorPage (#17); widget palette + theme picker = placeholders only (#18, #19, #20, #21). **Architectural questions surfaced during build**: (a) background-click on cores — cores have no substrate/typography vocab; resolved by falling through to chrome editing (the only editable surface); documented inline; (b) inspector sections inline-vs-extracted choice — kept inline this iteration; each section is ~50-80 LOC and inline keeps the selection dispatcher visible in one place; future F-3 widget palette + F-5 polish may motivate extraction; (c) one-of-both-hooks mounted unconditionally — both `useFocusCoreDraft` AND `useFocusTemplateDraft` mount, each with `null | id` based on subject kind; the unbound hook is a no-op per the hook's own contract; alternative (Suspense or conditional hook mount) would violate React's rules-of-hooks; (d) the inspector's mode/empty + selection-kind dispatch is a 2×4 table; covered by the test matrix but worth keeping a close eye on as F-3 adds widget selection. **Next**: F-3 (widget palette + drag-to-canvas + accessory placement editing).

- **2026-05-18 — DECISIONS.md updated (uncommitted): filed two discovered-canon entries from F-1 + F-1.1** — Canon-update-only arc; no code changes. Two entries appended to `DECISIONS.md`: (1) "Cores are canonical-shared-across-verticals" — `focus_cores` has no `vertical` field; vertical attribution in operator-facing surfaces (Focus Builder tree) is derived from inheriting templates (vertical_default templates pin core to vertical; platform_default makes cross-vertical; zero-template cores fall into "Unclassified"). Implication: future builder UIs (Page/Document/Workflow) must derive vertical placement from inheriting templates, not from non-existent core fields. (2) "Template vertical is design-time-permanent" — `focus_templates.vertical` is immutable through `update_template`; cross-vertical migration requires two-step pattern (deactivate at old vertical + create at new vertical), idempotent on subsequent runs. Implication: future UI surfaces must not expose "change vertical" as inline edit on a template — the operation is structurally a "create new in target + deactivate old" workflow. Reference impl: F-1.1's seed migration code at `backend/scripts/seed_focus_template_inheritance.py`. Active arc → no active arc, canon update only. **Files modified**: `DECISIONS.md` (+38 lines, format-adapted to match existing prose-paragraph + date-prefix style), `STATE.md` (this entry). No code files touched. No tests required.

- **2026-05-18 — Sub-arc E-1.1 shipped (uncommitted) — E-1 verification follow-ups closed** — Post-E-1 visual verification surfaced two real findings the E-1 build missed. **Finding 1: scheduling-kanban-core chrome only partially canonical.** E-1 shipped delta updates (corner_radius 100→70, padding_token space-6→space-3, backdrop_blur 42→44) but preserved pre-E-1 values on the other four chrome fields: preset `card` (canonical: `frosted`), elevation 37 (canonical: 50), background_token `surface-elevated` (canonical: `surface-frosted`), border_token `None` (canonical: `border-subtle`). E-1.1 re-seeds with FULL canonical chrome state — all 7 fields explicit — bumping core to v9. **Finding 2: Tier 1 editor preview pane atmosphere not mockup-canonical.** Pre-E-1.1 the canvas painted a warm-amber/copper diagonal gradient (`linear-gradient(135deg, #f9d9a6 0%, #e9b27e 30%, #c97d52 60%, #9C5640 100%)`) plus a 30%-opacity 45° repeating stripe overlay — Tier 1 editor chrome that diverged from the canonical mockup. Replaced with the four-layer canonical mockup composition: three radial gradients (warm cream rgba(252,220,180,0.55) at 15%/10%, soft pink rgba(220,170,200,0.40) at 85%/15%, cool blue rgba(180,200,220,0.45) at 50%/90%) over a vertical linear-gradient base (`#f7ebe0 → #f0dfd0`). Hardcoded directly on the editor's preview pane — NOT routed through substrate-resolver (locked decision 2: Tier 1 cores have no substrate vocabulary). Values mirror substrate-resolver's `morning-warm` preset at intensity 100 so operator-facing + admin-facing surfaces feel canon-matched; diagonal-stripe overlay removed for canonical fidelity. **(1) Seed re-shipped with full canonical chrome state** — `backend/scripts/seed_focus_template_inheritance.py`: SCHEDULING_KANBAN_CORE.chrome now specifies all 7 fields explicitly (`preset: "frosted", elevation: 50, corner_radius: 70, backdrop_blur: 44, background_token: "surface-frosted", border_token: "border-subtle", padding_token: "space-3"`). Drift-tolerant `_seed_core` detects content divergence and calls `update_core` to version-bump existing rows; previous v8 record preserved as `is_active=false`. **(2) Tier-2 template version-bump on stale core pin** — `_seed_template` extended with a new "force version-bump when `inherits_from_core_version` lags live core version" path. Rationale: `update_template` preserves the prior `inherits_from_core_version` (immutable through that surface — service-layer captures from the live active core only on `create_template`). The resolver always uses the active core regardless (locked decision 2), but C-2.3's lineage chrome reads `template.inherits_from_core_version` directly, so a stale stamp would display as "v1" in the editor even after the core moves to v9. The new branch calls `create_template` to trigger a version-bump that restamps `inherits_from_core_version` to live core.version on the deactivate-and-insert path. Idempotent: subsequent reruns short-circuit because the stamp matches. **(3) Tier 1 editor canvas atmosphere canonicalized** — `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/components/visual-editor/Tier1CoresEditor.tsx`: preview-pane `<section data-testid="tier1-preview">` `background` style replaced with the four-layer canonical composition; diagonal-stripe `<div aria-hidden>` overlay deleted; `isolation: isolate` added so the canvas establishes its own stacking context. Inline-style approach is deliberate per locked decision 2 (Tier 1 has no substrate vocabulary). **(4) Canonical mockup committed** — new `docs/design/canonical-mockups/funeral_scheduling_apple_pre_liquid_glass.html` (a self-contained four-column kanban skeleton with frosted cards demonstrating the substrate + chrome + typography canon, no build step, opens directly in a browser) + `docs/design/canonical-mockups/README.md` explaining the canonical-mockup convention. Authoritative reference for the morning-warm substrate composition, frosted chrome preset values, and frosted-text typography preset values — referenced by E-1 and E-1.1. **Tests**: new `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/components/visual-editor/Tier1CoresEditor.test.tsx` (2 tests) asserts the four-layer canonical composition is present on the canvas + the pre-E-1.1 warm-amber gradient is absent (JSDom normalizes hex to rgb so assertions check both normalized stops `rgb(247, 235, 224)` / `rgb(240, 223, 208)` and explicit hex absence). **Gates**: full vitest **196 files / 2715 tests + 1 todo passing** (+1 file / +2 tests vs E-1's 195/2713); tsc clean; vite build 4.98s, bundle unchanged within ±2%. Backend 264/264 across 9 focus_template_inheritance test files (full backend suite green). **LOC**: ~115 changed (seed ~50 net delta with new version-bump branch + comment block; Tier1CoresEditor ~25 (canvas style replace + overlay delete); new test file ~80; mockup HTML ~210 + README ~22 = docs ~232) — well under the ~300-600 midpoint, comfortably under 900 worst case. **No backend service changes, no schema changes, no migrations, no resolver module changes, no Tier 2 editor surfaces touched, no canon doc edits beyond STATE.md, Frosted Scribe not touched per locked decision 7.** Migration head unchanged: `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`. **Locked decisions honored**: full canonical chrome state replacement (#1); editor preview pane canonical composition hardcoded, NOT routed through substrate-resolver (#2); scheduling-fh `inherits_from_core_version` auto-bumps to new active version via the new seed branch (#3); substrate-resolver morning-warm unchanged (#4); no backend schema or migration (#5); resolver modules untouched (#6); Frosted Scribe not touched (#7); canonical mockup HTML committed (#8). **Open architectural question surfaced**: the `_seed_template` version-bump branch is a workaround for `update_template` preserving the prior `inherits_from_core_version` — clean long-term path is either (a) extending `update_template` to optionally restamp from live core, or (b) adding a dedicated `restamp_core_version_pin` service. Not blocking; the seed-only workaround is correct for E-1.1's surface but if multiple templates inherit from the same core in future, each will need a similar code path. **Next**: full Focus Builder UI restructuring (vertical-grouped left rail nav, selection-driven inspector, widget palette, theme preset switcher in right rail, breadcrumb context, right-bar cleanup, drag widgets into Tier 2, Tier 3 work) — explicitly out of scope for E-1.1.

- **2026-05-18 — Sub-arc E-1 shipped (uncommitted) — mockup-canonical-defaults arc closed** — Post-C-2 verification revealed three findings: (1) Tier 2 templates didn't inherit Tier 1's exact look on creation — substrate-resolver's `morning-warm` preset at intensity 70 produced a flat cream wash rather than the canonical warm sunrise gradient; (2) Tier 1 scheduling-kanban-core chrome diverged from mockup card chrome (corner_radius 37 / padding_token space-6 / no backdrop_blur vs. mockup 70 / space-3 / 44); (3) new Tier 2 templates via the C-2.2c modal started with empty substrate/typography rather than canonical mockup defaults. E-1 closes all three. **(1) Substrate-resolver morning-warm canonical** — `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/lib/visual-editor/substrate-resolver.ts`: `morning-warm` preset rebuilt as a four-layer composition. Three radial gradients (warm cream `rgba(252, 220, 180, α)` ellipse-at-15%-10%; pink `rgba(220, 170, 200, α)` ellipse-at-85%-15%; cool blue `rgba(180, 200, 220, α)` ellipse-at-50%-90%) over a token-bindable linear-gradient base (`accent_token_1` top stop → `base_token` bottom stop; default `surface-elevated` → `surface-base`). Radial alphas at intensity 100 are canonical 0.55 / 0.40 / 0.45; intensity scales linearly to 0 (no radials). Radial colors, positions, ellipse sizes are HARDCODED — not operator-tunable. `accent_token_2` is unused for morning-warm. SUBSTRATE_PRESETS entry updated: `intensity: 100` default + `base_token: surface-base` + `accent_token_1: surface-elevated` + `accent_token_2: null`. Other presets preserve the legacy two-stop diagonal composition via fall-through branch. Resolver function signature unchanged (`resolveSubstrateStyle(view, tokens) → CSSProperties`). **(2) Backend create-time defaults** — new `backend/app/services/focus_template_inheritance/defaults.py` canonicalizes `DEFAULT_CHROME_OVERRIDES = {}` (cascade chrome from core unchanged), `DEFAULT_SUBSTRATE = {preset: "morning-warm", intensity: 100, base_token: "surface-base", accent_token_1: "surface-elevated", accent_token_2: None}`, `DEFAULT_TYPOGRAPHY = {preset: "frosted-text", heading_weight: 600, body_weight: 500, heading_color_token: "content-strong", body_color_token: "content-base"}`. `focus_templates_service.create_template` calls `is_empty_blob(blob)` (True for None or `{}`) on each — empty-or-null populates the canonical default; any key-present mapping (even `{preset: None}`) is treated as explicit operator intent and respected verbatim. `update_template` semantics unchanged. **(3) Seed alignment** — `backend/scripts/seed_focus_template_inheritance.py`: scheduling-kanban-core chrome bumped from `{"preset": "card"}` to `{"preset": "card", "corner_radius": 70, "padding_token": "space-3", "backdrop_blur": 44}` — explicit overrides on top of the `card` preset stamp the mockup-canonical values at the row level. scheduling-fh template bumped to fully-explicit canonical mockup defaults matching DEFAULT_SUBSTRATE + DEFAULT_TYPOGRAPHY; chrome_overrides explicitly `{}` (cascade from core unchanged). Seed is drift-tolerant: `_seed_core` + `_seed_template` detect content divergence on rerun and call `update_core` / `update_template` to version-bump existing rows; previous version preserved as `is_active=false`. Re-running on unmodified seed is a clean no-op. **Frosted Scribe template intentionally NOT seeded** — no such template exists in the codebase today; the prompt's reference appears aspirational. Surfaced. **Tests**: new `backend/tests/test_focus_template_inheritance_e1_defaults.py` (12 tests across 2 classes) covers defaults.py shape + create_template wiring. Five existing tests updated for E-1 contract change: `TestTemplateServiceSubstrate::test_create_default_empty_substrate` + `TestTemplateServiceTypography::test_create_default_empty_typography` now expect canonical defaults; admin API `test_template_response_includes_all_substrate_fields` + `test_template_response_includes_all_typography_fields` updated to expect canonical mockup default values; resolver "empty at both tiers → None" tests (substrate + typography) updated to null the column out directly post-create (simulates pre-E1 seeded rows). Substrate-resolver vitest expanded from 6 to 13 tests: morning-warm intensity 100/50/0; token-binding to linear base stops; other-presets-unchanged regression. **Gates**: backend pytest 241/241 green across 8 focus template inheritance test files; frontend tsc clean; vitest 2712/2714 passing (1 failure is pre-existing flaky `Tier2TemplatesEditor.test.tsx` `preview-card chrome preset updates live when chrome pill clicked` — fails identically with E-1 absent, passes when isolated; not introduced by E-1); vite build clean 5.06s, bundle unchanged within ±2%. **Out of scope per spec**: card content, Tier 1 editor preview CSS, other substrate/typography/chrome presets, right-bar cleanup, widget palette, Tier 3 work. **Migration head unchanged** — pure JSONB content alignment via service-layer versioning.

- **2026-05-18 — Sub-arc C-2.3 shipped (uncommitted) — C-2 sub-arc canonically complete** — Final sub-sub-arc of C-2. Ships the inheritance-surfacing layer + URL consolidation polish that closes C-2 end-to-end. **(1) Per-row inheritance indicators in the Tier 2 inspector** — `PropertyRow` (in `PropertyPanel.tsx`) extended with optional `inheritanceSource?: "explicit" | { tier: string } | null` and `onReset?: () => void` props. Inherited rows render dimmed value (opacity 60) + a brass-toned "↑ inherited from <tier>" mono caption below the row; explicit rows render full-opacity. Driven ENTIRELY by the resolver's `sources.*_sources` provenance (locked decision #4) — Tier2TemplatesEditor calls a new `focusTemplatesService.resolve({template_slug, vertical})` and maps each tier string ("tier1"/"tier2"/"tier3"/null) to a `PropertyRowInheritance`: `"tier1"` → `{tier: "Tier 1 core"}` (chrome only — substrate + typography are tier-1-free by design per resolver); `"tier2"/"tier3"` → `"explicit"`; `null` → no decoration. Existing PropertyRow consumers (Tier1CoresEditor, InheritedCoreInspectorPanel) untouched — neutral rows render exactly as before when no `inheritanceSource` is supplied. **(2) Reset-to-inherited ↺ affordance** — hover-only RotateCcw icon button rendered to the right of the value block, opacity 0 at rest → 100 on row hover or button focus; only renders when row is "explicit" AND `onReset` is wired. New hook methods: `resetChromeOverridesField(fieldName)` / `resetSubstrateField(fieldName)` / `resetTypographyField(fieldName)` on `useFocusTemplateDraft`. Each removes the named key via `delete next[fieldName]` (object identity preserved when key absent — short-circuit prevents needless save trigger), then calls `queueSave` to fire the standard 300ms debounced PUT. Reset is dirty-positive: `isDirty=true` momentarily, snaps back to `false` after the round-trip. Per locked decisions #5/#8 Tier 1 cores editor gets NO inheritance indicators or reset (cascade root). **(3) Tier indicator pill** — brass-toned chip ("Tier 1" / "Tier 2") rendered in FocusEditorPage's top bar adjacent to the "Focuses" title, gated on `(tier===1 && selectedCoreId) || (tier===2 && selectedTemplateId)` so the chip only appears when there's a target to attribute the tier to. `bg-accent-subtle text-accent` with mono font and `data-tier` discriminator for tests. **(4) Interactive lineage chrome** — the existing "Inherits from: X (Tier 1 v<N>)" text in FocusEditorPage's top bar is now a button. Click opens InheritedCoreInspectorPanel (same panel as canvas placement click per locked decision #15); visual unchanged at rest, subtle accent-subtle hover treatment. Dirty-state confirm-before-leave flow inherits from C-2.2c automatically — the panel handles it. - **2026-05-15 — Sub-arc C-2.1.3 shipped (uncommitted)** — Closes the misdiagnosed dirty-state-clear bug from C-2.1.2. The real root cause was not JSONB key-order (C-2.1.2's hypothesis) but null-stripping in the backend serializer: `_core_to_response` did `dict(row.chrome or {})` which carries only the keys actually present on the row, while the frontend draft populates the full 7-field chrome canonical shape (some values null) as the user touches sliders. Response had 4 keys, draft had 7 → C-2.1.2's `deepEqualChrome` (key-order-tolerant but key-set-strict) returned `!equal` forever → "Unsaved" indicator stuck post-save. Production DevTools inspection confirmed: PUT response chrome blob carried `{preset, elevation, corner_radius, backdrop_blur}` — missing `background_token`, `border_token`, `padding_token`. C-2.1.2's regression test passed for the wrong reason: the mock returned chrome with the same key set as the draft (key-order swapped only), never reproducing production's sparse-key shape. **Backend fix (Option B — clean contract)**: `_core_to_response` + `_template_to_response` (chrome_overrides + substrate + typography) now normalize via a new `_normalize_blob(stored, canonical_fields)` helper. Canonical field sets imported from `chrome_validation.CHROME_FIELDS` (7), `substrate_validation.SUBSTRATE_FIELDS` (5), `typography_validation.TYPOGRAPHY_FIELDS` (5) — already cleanly exported by B-3.5 / B-4 / B-5 validators, no inlining needed. Every response carries the full canonical key set with explicit `null` for unset fields. Database storage stays as-is (null/missing fields stay however JSONB writes them); only the API response is normalized. NO migration. **Frontend fix (Option A — defensive)**: `deepEqualChrome` in `useFocusCoreDraft.ts` rewritten to treat missing-key and explicit-null/undefined-value as semantically equivalent — `{a:1, b:null}` deep-equals `{a:1}`. Union-of-keys iteration; both null/undefined branches short-circuit to `true`. Defensive against any current or future backend serializer that drops null fields. **C-2.1.2's helper kept** (per scope rule "do not remove or revert"); comment updated to reflect C-2.1.3 semantics (key-order-AND-key-set-tolerant). **C-2.1.2's regression test kept-and-improved**: original "key-order swap" test still passes (correct in spirit); 3 new C-2.1.3 tests added that REPRODUCE the production bug (mock response chrome has FEWER keys than draft) — pre-C-2.1.3 implementation would FAIL on those; post-fix all pass. Plus a "missing key == explicit null" equivalence test and a "normalized full-shape response" test (post-backend-fix path). **Tests: 7 new backend** in `test_focus_template_inheritance_admin_api.py` covering core empty-chrome → 7 explicit nulls, core partial update → 7 keys with 1 valued + 6 null, GET round-trip preserves full shape, template chrome_overrides normalized, template substrate normalized (5 keys), template typography normalized (5 keys), list endpoint normalizes every row. **5 pre-existing backend tests updated** in `test_focus_template_inheritance_chrome.py` (1) + `_substrate.py` (2) + `_typography.py` (2) — exact-equality assertions on response blobs aligned to the new normalized shape; these tests were the contract for the pre-C-2.1.3 sparse shape, now updated with explanatory comments. **3 new frontend tests** in `useFocusCoreDraft.test.tsx` (1) sparse-response-vs-7-field-draft regression that reproduces production bug, (2) missing-key/explicit-null equivalence for dirty check, (3) normalized full-shape response path after backend fix. Backend regression: 228/228 focus_template_inheritance suite (chrome 54 + substrate 47 + typography 49 + admin_api 17 + service 50 + session_aware 9 + session_aware_templates 13 — including 7 new C-2.1.3 admin_api tests + 5 pre-existing aligned). Frontend regression: vitest 2589/2589 + 1 todo passing (20/20 in useFocusCoreDraft.test.tsx); tsc clean; vite build 5.89s. LOC: ~50 backend production-code (route serializer +25 incl. new `_normalize_blob` helper + 3 imports + 2 call sites; existing validators untouched) + ~190 backend tests (7 new + 5 modified) + ~30 frontend production-code (hook deepEqualChrome rewrite) + ~110 frontend tests = ~380 total (within ~250-400 midpoint). No migration. No schema changes. No canon doc edits. **Diagnostic root-cause confirmation**: the build prompt's diagnosis stood up — the production response WAS missing 3 chrome keys, draft DID carry all 7, and C-2.1.2's helper DID return `!equal` on sparse-key response. Hypothesis confirmed end-to-end. **Deferred per scope**: C-2.2 (next dispatch — Tier 2 templates editor); edge-panel templates response normalization (apply same pattern when edge-panel session-aware ships); new session-aware semantics; new substrate vocabularies; audit log substrate; resolver changes. Migration head unchanged: `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`.

- **2026-05-15 — Sub-arc C-2.1.2 shipped (uncommitted)** — Mixed backend + frontend fix closing three issues before C-2.2 dispatches: (1) session-aware update semantics for `focus_templates` (Tier 2 — mirrors C-2.1.1 verbatim), (2) resolver slug-vs-UUID bug — live cascade restored by following active core BY SLUG instead of the template's stored `inherits_from_core_id`, (3) `useFocusCoreDraft` dirty-state-clear bug — "Unsaved" indicator was sticking after successful save because `JSON.stringify` equality is key-order-sensitive and PostgreSQL JSONB does not preserve insertion order on round-trip. **Migration `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`** adds `last_edit_session_id UUID NULL` + `last_edit_session_at TIMESTAMPTZ NULL` to focus_templates; reversible; mirrors r102's columns on focus_cores. **`update_template` becomes session-aware**: in-place mutation within 5-min window matching session_id (or first-touch on never-stamped row); version-bump for no-token / expired / different-token / no-session paths; INACTIVE target → new `StaleTemplateVersionError(inactive_id, slug, scope, vertical, active_id)` → **HTTP 410 Gone** with structured `detail: {message, inactive_template_id, active_template_id, slug, scope, vertical}` so frontend swaps its local id + retries under the SAME session token. `TemplateUpdateRequest.edit_session_id` added; `TemplateResponse.last_edit_session_id` + `last_edit_session_at` added. **Resolver slug-based active core lookup** (locked Option A, silent transparent resolve per α): two new helpers `get_core_slug_by_id` + `get_active_core_by_slug` in focus_cores_service; resolver does `slug_by_id(template.inherits_from_core_id) → active_core_by_slug(slug)` rather than direct PK lookup of stored id. When stored UUID is still active, slug lookup returns same row (regression-safe); when bumped, slug lookup returns NEW active row (closes live-cascade bug). Both lookups indexed (PK + partial-unique `ix_focus_cores_active_slug` from r96) — perceptible-impact zero. Orphan slug (would only happen via manual DB intervention bypassing partial-unique) raises `FocusTemplateNotFound` with descriptive message. **`EDIT_SESSION_WINDOW_SECONDS` lifted to shared `app/services/focus_template_inheritance/constants.py`** — single canonical source; cores + templates + future edge-panel session-aware semantics all import from there. `__init__.py` re-exports preserved public surface unchanged. **Frontend dirty-state-clear fix**: introduced narrow recursive `deepEqualChrome(a, b)` (key-order-independent, handles primitives + plain objects + arrays) in `useFocusCoreDraft.ts`; `isDirty` switched from `JSON.stringify(...)` inequality to `useMemo(() => !deepEqualChrome(draft, savedSnapshot), [draft, savedSnapshot])`. Root cause was hypothesis (b) variant — PostgreSQL JSONB round-trip reorders object keys; backend returned `{ elevation: 75, preset: "card" }` when draft was `{ preset: "card", elevation: 75 }` — JSON.stringify produced different strings → `isDirty = true` forever → "Auto-saved Xs ago" never appeared. **Tests: 13 new backend** in `test_focus_template_inheritance_session_aware_templates.py` across 3 classes (TestTemplateSessionAwareUpdate × 10, TestTemplateApiStaleReturns410 × 2, TestMigrationR103 × 1) + **4 new backend** in `test_focus_template_inheritance_service.py::TestResolverSlugBasedLookup` (regression slug-when-active, new behavior slug-after-bump, orphan raises, in-place propagation regression) + **2 new frontend** in `useFocusCoreDraft.test.tsx` (dirty clears on key-order-mismatch round-trip; dirty re-appears on subsequent update). Backend prior-arc regression: 70/70 across session_aware (29) + service (37 + appended 4) + admin_api (4). Adjacent focus_* tests: 164/164 across chrome + substrate + typography + schema + compositions. Frontend regression: vitest 2586/2586 + 1 todo passing; tsc clean; vite build 5.39s; main bundle 5,998,380 bytes = +440 bytes / +0.007% vs C-2.1.1 baseline 5,997,940 (well within ±2% gate). LOC: ~210 backend production-code (service +154, schema +8, migration +70, route +27, model +15, __init__ +7, constants +25, resolver +35) + ~610 backend tests (new file 489 + appended 121) + ~60 frontend production-code (hook) + ~63 frontend tests = ~1,150 total (within ~700-1,000 midpoint, comfortably under worst-case 1,300). **Resolver performance**: 2 indexed B-tree hits vs 1 PK hit — ~50-200µs added latency in unmeasured-but-typical territory; the partial-unique `ix_focus_cores_active_slug` makes the second lookup as cheap as the PK; no measurement script added (over-engineered for the change). **Deferred per Out-of-Scope**: C-2.2 Tier 2 templates editor (next dispatch); edge-panel session-aware (deferred); ResolvedFocus drift signaling (Option β deferred); audit log infrastructure; explicit "Publish v2" UI; multi-tab conflict detection beyond 410-retry; background cleanup of stale session_id rows; resolver caching. **Recommendation**: C-2.2 can now safely build the Tier 2 templates editor knowing scrub-session auto-save will mutate in place + the resolver will surface in-place mutations across all dependent compositions without staleness. Migration head: `r102_focus_cores_edit_session` → `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`.

- **2026-05-15 — Sub-arc C-2.1.1 shipped (uncommitted)** — Session-aware update semantics for `focus_cores` closes the version-bump-on-every-scrub bug from C-2.1. C-2.1's `useFocusCoreDraft` 300ms debounced auto-save was producing ~30+ version-bumps during a single elevation-slider drag because B-1's `update_core` versioned on every successful write; after the first save the frontend held a now-inactive UUID and subsequent saves returned 409. The fix: updates carrying an `edit_session_id` UUID v4 token that match the row's `last_edit_session_id` within 5 minutes (`EDIT_SESSION_WINDOW_SECONDS=300`) mutate in place — version unchanged, `updated_at` bumps, `last_edit_session_at` advances; row id stays the same so the frontend never goes stale. Updates outside the window OR with a different token version-bump per the B-1 behavior. Updates without any token version-bump (B-1 backward-compat preserved verbatim). **First-touch semantics**: when an update arrives with a token AND the row has never been session-stamped (`last_edit_session_id IS NULL`), the update mutates in place + sets the pointer — without this branch the FIRST update of every editor session would version-bump and the scrub-session would still produce one stray version per session. Migration `r102_focus_cores_edit_session` adds two columns to `focus_cores`: `last_edit_session_id UUID NULL` + `last_edit_session_at TIMESTAMPTZ NULL` (reversible; downgrade drops both, no data backfill needed since NULL is the correct "no active session" state). New `StaleCoreVersionError` exception carries `inactive_id` + `slug` + `active_id`; route layer translates to **HTTP 410 Gone** with structured `detail: {message, inactive_core_id, active_core_id, slug}` per **Spec-Override decision (Sonnet locked) option (i)** — preserves the addressing contract and surfaces staleness explicitly rather than silently redirecting. Frontend hook generates a UUID v4 token via `crypto.randomUUID()` (with Math.random fallback for test envs) when `coreId` transitions null → real OR switches between two real values; preserved across re-renders for the same coreId; cleared when coreId returns to null; intentionally NOT persisted across page reloads (page reload = fresh session). On 410 Gone the hook reads `active_core_id` from the error body, swaps its internal `activeCoreIdRef`, and retries the save once under the SAME session token — the scrub keeps going without visible interruption. `CoreUpdateRequest` gains `edit_session_id: str | None` (≤36 chars, optional). `CoreResponse` gains `last_edit_session_id` + `last_edit_session_at` for client telemetry. Tests: **16 new backend** in `test_focus_template_inheritance_session_aware.py` across 4 classes — `TestSessionAwareUpdate` × 10 (in-place mutate, consecutive same-session, cross-session bump, stale-window bump, no-token bump, unset-field preservation, session_at advance, stale-inactive raises, no-new-row, chrome persistence), `TestSessionAwareCascade` × 2 (in-place mutation flows through resolver without re-versioning templates; many in-place edits during one session keep template row at version 1), `TestApiStaleCoreReturns410` × 2 (410 body shape; session round-trip), `TestMigrationR102` × 1 (columns exist + populate). **6 new frontend** in `useFocusCoreDraft.test.tsx` (token generation, preserved across re-renders, refreshed on coreId switch, cleared on null, included in PUT payload, 410 retry path). Backend regression: 241/241 across focus_template_inheritance (188) + edge_panel_inheritance (24) + focus_compositions (29). Pre-existing B-1 version-bump tests (`test_update_versions`, `test_update_cannot_target_inactive`) preserved verbatim because they don't supply session tokens — version-bump path unchanged. Frontend: 15/15 useFocusCoreDraft tests pass (9 original + 6 new); tsc clean; vite build 5.46s; main bundle 5,997,940 bytes = +870 / +0.014% vs C-2.1 baseline 5,997,070 (well within ±2% gate). LOC: ~290 backend (service +130, schema +12, migration +50, route +30, model +15, __init__ +3, tests ~480 raw but ~280 effective service-test) + ~280 frontend (hook +120, service +30, tests +130) = ~570 production + ~610 tests = ~1,180 total (within ~600-900 midpoint, just under worst-case 1,200). **Deferred items**: (a) extending the same semantics to `focus_templates` (Tier 2) — likely the right call once C-2.2 ships a Tier 2 editor with auto-save, but scope-deferred to a follow-up sub-arc (call it C-2.1.2 or fold into C-2.2's slider-scrub work); (b) same for `edge_panel_templates` (B-1.5 territory); (c) explicit "Publish v2" UI affordance for deliberate version creation; (d) audit log capture of session events (no audit substrate for focus_cores exists yet); (e) session-token persistence across page reloads (intentional fresh-session contract); (f) multi-tab editing conflict detection; (g) telemetry on session-reuse rate. **Recommendation**: extend to `focus_templates` BEFORE C-2.2's Tier 2 editor ships — same auto-save pattern will produce the same bloat. Migration head: `r101_typography_substrate` → `r102_focus_cores_edit_session`.

## Active arc

- Arc name: Focus Template Inheritance (sub-arcs A → B → C → D → E → F)
- Current phase: **Sub-arc FF-3 closed (this commit, 2026-05-20) — drag-to-move on the free-form Focus canvas. First operator-interactive FF sub-arc. `FreeFormPlacedWidget` now wraps in @dnd-kit's `useDraggable`; positioning style (position:absolute / left / top / width / height / zIndex) moved up one DOM level to the new draggable wrapper at `data-testid="focus-builder-freeform-placed-widget-draggable"` so chrome + selection + click + keyboard activation stay UNTOUCHED on `PlacedWidgetCore` per the "do not touch core" constraint. `FocusBuilderPage.handleDragEnd` extended with an FF-3 branch: drag id matches `free-form-placed-widget:<placement-id>` → lookup placement via `flattenFreeFormPlacements(rowsDraft)` → apply `delta.x/y` via new pure helper `computeDragMoveCommit(...)` → canvas-bounded Q-14 clamp → fire `templateHook.updateWidget(id, { x, y })` through FF-1's positioning-field-routing path (no new hook surface). PointerSensor activation threshold tightened from F-3's 6px → canonical 3px per Q-9 (click/drag disambiguation); new KeyboardSensor added per Q-40 mitigation enabling integration-test coverage via Space-to-grab + arrow-nudge + Space-to-drop (document is the keydown listener target per @dnd-kit/core after activation; activation fires onKeyDown on the activator). Drag-active visual feedback: `cursor: grab` idle → `grabbing` active, opacity 0.85 + level-2 shadow + z-index lift during gesture; resets on drag-end. NO snap-to-alignment (FF-7), NO keyboard nudge outside drag-active (FF-7), NO resize (FF-4), NO z-index UX (FF-5), NO inspector positioning fields (FF-6). 1 new pure helper + 1 unit-test file + 2 component edits + 3 integration tests. `computeDragMoveCommit.test.ts` covers 9 Q-14 clamp cases pure-function. Cross-side render+save assertion in integration test verifies BOTH the wrapper's inline-style `left` value advances past initial AND the PUT body's placement.x is updated; canvas-edge clamp test seeds at x=900 (canvas 1200 - widget 240 = max 960) and asserts saved x ≤ 960. Verify-against-pre-fix discipline applied: reverting `templateHook.updateWidget(...)` to a no-op fails BOTH integration tests (save side: `update` not called; render side: `left` unchanged from 100); restored → both pass. Existing FF-2 positioning unit tests retargeted from `focus-builder-placed-widget` (PlacedWidgetCore's outer) to `focus-builder-freeform-placed-widget-draggable` (new wrapper) — same operator-observable contract, one level up. (b) KeyboardSensor in JSDOM works in practice but requires (i) target the activator (draggable element) for the activating Space keydown — matches `event.target === activator` activator-handler check, (ii) target `document` for subsequent arrow nudges and the committing Space — KeyboardSensor's move/end listener lives on `getOwnerDocument(target)` per @dnd-kit's `attach()`, (iii) advance fake timers ~10ms after activation because the listener is attached inside a `setTimeout(0)`. Documenting this pattern for FF-4 + future arc reuse.**

- Prior phase (FF-1 closed 2026-05-20 at `10321ed`): FF-series foundation. Backend `_validate_placement` extended with free-form dispatch: placements carrying any of `x` / `y` / `width` / `height` validate as pixel-positioned free-form (positive numbers, bounds-checked against `canvas_config.width` / `.height` with default 1200×800); placements without those fields continue validating as F-series grid (`starting_column` + `column_span`). Optional `z_index` integer; min width/height = 1 px at validator (per-widget min/max is FF-4's resize-gesture concern). Template-level shape consistency check rejects mixed-shape templates with 422 + clear message after individual placement validation. `create_template` stamps default canvas_config `{width: 1200, height: 800}` ONLY when caller passes empty/null config — explicit keys respected verbatim (matches E-1 empty-blob discipline for chrome / substrate / typography). `update_template` reorders canvas_config computation BEFORE row validation so free-form bounds check against the operator's intended dimensions on this save (not prior version's). Frontend `WidgetPlacement` interface gains optional `x` / `y` / `width` / `height` / `z_index` fields alongside now-optional `column_start` / `column_span`. `_placement-adapter.ts` detects shape by field presence and translates 1:1 for pixel coords (no off-by-one — Q-25 locked) while preserving F-3.1a's 1↔0-indexed column translation for grid placements. Hook `addWidget(slug, position?)` accepts both field families (free-form when any of x/y/width/height supplied; otherwise grid F-3 default). `updateWidget(id, partial)` routes positioning-field keys to top-level placement fields and everything else to chrome merge — same mutator handles drag/resize commits (FF-3/4) and F-3 chrome merges through a single code path. ZERO Alembic migrations (Q-23 pure-JSONB extension); ZERO canvas substrate / inspector / palette / theme-picker changes — operators see no visible difference.
