Observed symptoms (Playwright screenshot, post-`0623ed3` deploy):
  - Top bar displays "Vertical: dispatch" — something is reading the raw `:vertical` URL param without going through `disambiguateStudioLive`
  - Dev banner shows `Page: unmapped:/bridgeable-admin/studio/live/dispatch/funeral-schedule`
  - Pulse/Home overview surface renders instead of `FuneralSchedulePage`

  Follow-up #4's verticals-aware disambiguation shipped cleanly (vitest 2476/2476 pass, including 18 new disambiguation tests) but did not change the rendered output, indicating a consumer outside `StudioLiveModeWrap` and `TenantUserPicker` is reading the URL directly. Likely candidates: `StudioScopeSwitcher` (renders "Vertical: dispatch"), `StudioShell`-level dispatch outside the nested Routes block, or an `EditModeDispatcher` path that matches `:vertical = "dispatch"` ahead of the Live mode Routes.

  Six fixes have been attempted in service of Gates 14 and 22 across the Studio 1a-i sequence (A2 redirect, R-2.x.1 universal-relative-paths, follow-up #2 auth gate, follow-up #3 router topology + picker pickup-and-replay, follow-up #4 verticals disambiguation). Each fix has shipped clean and tested correctly at the unit level, but Gates 14/22 remain red. The diagnostic gap is that chat-driven static analysis has not been sufficient — each fix has been based on a plausible-sounding diagnosis that turned out incomplete. Resolution requires hands-on DevTools debugging on the deployed staging app: open `/bridgeable-admin/studio/live/dispatch/funeral-schedule` while logged in, walk the React component tree, find what is rendering "Vertical: dispatch" and what is mounting the Pulse overview, identify the consumer that bypasses `disambiguateStudioLive`, fix in one shot with evidence.

  Not blocking the Studio platform thesis. Operators can navigate Studio, edit themes, focus authoring, workflows, edge panels. The redirect chain works. The shell mounts correctly. 53 of 56 Playwright gates pass. Gates 14/22 affect a specific click-to-edit path on deep tenant routes — material, but downstream of the Studio shell's substrate work.

## Recently shipped (rolling, last 10)

0. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc FF-2 — canvas substrate replacement (free-form rendering ships visibly)** (uncommitted, 2026-05-20). First FF-series sub-arc producing operator-visible change. Canvas substrate now detects template shape per `detectTemplateShape(rowsDraft)` and routes to one of two layers: `WidgetFreeFormLayer` (absolute-positioned, FF-2 new) or `WidgetRowsLayer` (CSS-grid, F-3 preserved). `PlacedWidgetCore` extracted as shared inner wrapper per Q-29 — owns chrome resolution (DEFAULT_WIDGET_CHROME ← placement.chrome via `chrome-resolver` pipeline), selection chrome (brass outline on selected), click + keyboard handlers, widget component render via registry. Both positioning shells (`PlacedWidget` for grid, `FreeFormPlacedWidget` for free-form) are thin layout-only adapters consuming the shared core. Outer `data-testid="focus-builder-placed-widget"` preserved on the wrapper (F-3.1c selector continuity); new `data-testid="focus-builder-placed-widget-core"` added at the inner div as the FF-2 operator-observable assertion anchor per the 2026-05-20 late-evening canon. Inherited core renders at Q-20 canonical position inside `WidgetFreeFormLayer`: `core_width = canvas_width * (default_column_span/12)`, `core_x = (canvas_width - core_width)/2`, `core_y = 40`. Drop coordinate translation in `handleDragEnd`: pulls cursor from dnd-kit's `activatorEvent.clientX/Y + delta` minus layer-rect offset, computes pixel position via new pure helper `computeFreeFormDropPosition({cursorX, cursorY, width, height, canvasWidth, canvasHeight})` applying Q-4 centering (`x = cursorX - width/2`, `y = cursorY - height/2`) + Q-14 canvas-bounded clamp; resolves per-widget default size via new `getFreeFormDefaultDimensions(slug)` (registry lookup with `FREE_FORM_DEFAULT_DIMENSIONS` 320×180 platform fallback). Empty templates default to free-form per Q-27 — every new Focus template authored after FF-2 ships is free-form. `RegistrationMetadata.canvasMetadata` extended with optional `freeFormDefaultDimensions` + `freeFormMinDimensions` (pixels) alongside existing grid-cell `defaultDimensions` + `minDimensions`. Day Strip + Today Pin + Map widget seeds backfilled: 240×120 / 240×120 / 400×400 free-form defaults. Defensive `canvas_config` fallback to 1200×800 honored throughout (Q-2 refinement from FF-1) — partial canvas_configs carrying only `{gap_size: 4}` render correctly. Selection model carries over unchanged from F-2: `{kind: "widget", id}` discriminator works for both grid and free-form placements. Tests shipped: PlacedWidgetCore (9 unit), PlacedWidget regression (5 unit), FreeFormPlacedWidget (7 unit), WidgetFreeFormLayer (9 unit), FocusBuilderCanvas FF-2 extension (10 unit covering detectTemplateShape + flattenFreeFormPlacements + computeFreeFormDropPosition + free-form layer render + grid regression + defensive fallback), FocusBuilderPage FF-2 integration (3 page-level cross-side tests covering free-form render through full mount + grid regression + selection wiring). Operator-observable canon honored: every integration assertion targets inline style values at rendered elements (e.g., `expect(styleAttr).toMatch(/position:\s*absolute/i)` + `/left:\s*100px/i`); pure-function unit tests cover Q-4 + Q-14 drop logic so JSDOM weakness on dnd-kit pointer gestures per Q-40 doesn't block FF-2 — full drag-end Playwright coverage defers to FF-7. **Full frontend regression: 2965 vitest tests + 1 todo across 217 test files passing.** tsc clean. vite build clean (bundle 6,095 kB, within ±0.5% tolerance). Phase 1–FF-1 regression unaffected. FF-1 substrate (validator, adapter, hook helpers, WidgetPlacement interface) untouched per FF-2 scope. **Architectural surprises: zero** — PlacedWidgetCore extraction was mechanical Q-29 (c) decomposition; the cleanest seam was passing `outerStyle: React.CSSProperties` from positioning shells to the shared core so the chrome+selection+click layer stays byte-equivalent with F-3.1c's inline implementation while positioning becomes shape-aware. HEAD pre-flight verified `10321ed`. Foundation is in place for FF-3 drag-to-move via @dnd-kit KeyboardSensor.

1. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc FF-1 — free-form canvas foundation (validator + adapter extension)** (uncommitted, 2026-05-20). Foundation sub-arc of the FF-series (locked decisions Q-1 through Q-5 / Q-23 / Q-24 / Q-25 / Q-27 from `docs/investigations/2026-05-20-free-form-focus-canvas.md`). Backend `_validate_placement` now dispatches on placement-shape detection (field presence of `x` / `y` / `width` / `height` → free-form; otherwise grid). Free-form validation: positive numbers, bounds against `canvas_config.width` / `.height` (default 1200×800 — `DEFAULT_CANVAS_WIDTH` / `DEFAULT_CANVAS_HEIGHT` constants). Optional `z_index` integer; min width/height = 1 px (per-widget min/max is FF-4's resize-gesture concern). `is_core` discriminator works for both shapes; same component_kind+name match check as grid. Template-level shape consistency check fires AFTER per-placement validation — mixed-shape templates rejected with 422 + clear message. `create_template` stamps default canvas_config ONLY when caller passes empty/null config (E-1 empty-blob discipline preserved — explicit keys round-trip verbatim, so F-series test fixtures passing `{gap_size: 4}` aren't infill-stamped). `update_template` reorders canvas_config computation BEFORE row validation so free-form bounds check against operator's intent on THIS save. Frontend `WidgetPlacement` interface extended: `column_start` / `column_span` now optional; additive `x` / `y` / `width` / `height` / `z_index`. `_placement-adapter.ts` detects shape by field presence; free-form coords pass 1:1 (Q-25 — no off-by-one for pixels); grid retains 1↔0-indexed column translation. Hook `addWidget(slug, position?)` accepts BOTH field families and emits the matching placement shape (free-form when any positioning field supplied; otherwise grid F-3 default). `updateWidget(id, partial)` routes positioning-field keys (x/y/width/height/z_index/column_start/column_span) to top-level placement fields and remaining keys to chrome merge — single mutator handles future drag/resize commits (FF-3/4) AND existing F-3 chrome merges through one code path. **ZERO Alembic migrations** (Q-23 pure-JSONB extension; migration head stays `r103_focus_templates_edit_session`). **ZERO frontend canvas / inspector / palette / theme-picker changes** — FF-1 is invisible to operators. Existing seeded templates not migrated (Q-24 — they stay grid-shaped, validator continues accepting). Adapter pattern preserved without refactoring (Q-23 additive); validator extension was a clean additive branch. Operator-observable cross-side test canon not applicable — FF-1 has no render-side changes; tests are at validator + hook-state + adapter-translation level (per prompt's explicit carve-out). **27 new backend tests** in `test_focus_template_freeform_validation.py` across 6 test classes: TestFreeFormValidation (6 acceptance + is_core match/mismatch), TestFreeFormRejection (7 boundary + type rejections including bool-as-number defense), TestCanvasConfigDefaults (4 cases incl. constant sanity), TestCreateTemplateCanvasStamping (4 cases verifying empty-only stamping preserves E-1 discipline for partial canvas_config), TestGridShapeRegression (3 F-series invariants), TestMixedShapeRejection (3 cases incl. end-to-end via `create_template` API surface). **18 new frontend tests** across the two existing test files: 9 in `_placement-adapter.test.ts` (free-form emit, no grid-field leak, z_index emission, round-trip preservation, free-form backend read, grid regression, no field leak on backend read, backend→frontend→backend free-form round-trip, row-level multi-placement free-form round-trip) + 9 in `useFocusTemplateDraft.test.tsx` (addWidget free-form positioning storage, addWidget with z_index, addWidget without positioning preserves grid default, updateWidget key routing for mixed position+chrome partial, partial position update preserves other fields, save-side adapter integration emits positioning fields without grid leak, load-side adapter integration reads free-form payload into typed view). **Full backend regression: 297 focus-template tests passing**, no F-series regressions. **Full frontend regression: 2923 vitest tests + 1 todo across 213 test files passing**. tsc clean. Bundle delta: 6088.79 → 6089.81 kB = +1.02 kB / +0.017% (well within ±0.5%). 1. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc C-2.1.4 — dirty-state-clear bug DEFINITIVE fix via draftRef** (this commit, 2026-05-15). Third diagnosis of the same surface symptom; first one pinned by direct fiber-state inspection in production rather than static analysis. Root cause: `useFocusCoreDraft.save` had `draft` in its `useCallback` deps array → save's identity changed every render → the setTimeout queued in `updateDraft` captured a save function whose closure was already one event behind by the time the timer fired (300ms later). Result on a continuous scrub: every PUT persisted a value one scrub-step behind the actual draft. Wire-level evidence: every PUT 200, request matches response exactly. React state evidence (fiber walk): `draft = {elevation: 50}` (user's latest) but `savedSnapshot = {elevation: 49}` (one event behind, what was actually saved). `deepEqualChrome(draft, savedSnapshot)` correctly returned false; `isDirty` correctly stuck true; "Unsaved" indicator correctly never cleared. The bug was the saved value, not the comparison. Fix: canonical React stale-closure-in-callback-deps pattern. New `draftRef` synced via useEffect on every draft change; `save` reads `draftRef.current` for the PUT payload (latest committed draft, not closure); `draft` removed from save's `useCallback` deps → save's identity is now stable across draft changes. The setTimeout in updateDraft now captures a save that always reads the current draft via the ref when fired. Three-update race regression test (`save sends latest draft value not stale closure value`): fires updateDraft({elevation: 70}) → updateDraft({elevation: 72}) → updateDraft({elevation: 75}) without intervening waits, then verifies the single resulting save payload contains `elevation === 75` AND `isDirty === false` after the save resolves. Test verified to FAIL against pre-fix code with `expected 72 to be 75` (concrete confirmation it catches the race) and PASS against the fix. Prior C-2.1.2 + C-2.1.3 work preserved: deepEqualChrome's key-set-tolerance + null-equivalence + backend canonical full-shape response contract are all still correct + load-bearing for defense-in-depth. C-2.1.4 is the additive fix that closes the actual symptom. ~115 LOC (50 production + 65 test). Vitest: 2590/2590 + 1 todo (was 2589; +1 net new); 21/21 in useFocusCoreDraft suite. tsc clean. vite build 5.48s, main bundle 5,998,510 bytes (+1,440 / +0.024%). Backend untouched. **Lesson codified**: static-analysis diagnosis of React state bugs is high-false-positive when the bug involves timing + closure capture; fiber-state inspection in production is the right diagnostic tool for "saves succeed at wire level but UI shows wrong state" symptoms. Sub-arc C-2.2 (Tier 2 templates editor + three-section inspector + canvas adaptation) is the next dispatch — substrate is genuinely complete now, with three independent fixes (one true root cause + two defense-in-depth) producing a robust auto-save loop.
2. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc C-2.1.3 — dirty-state-clear bug REAL fix** (`f7bc67c`, 2026-05-15). Closes C-2.1.2's misdiagnosis. Production response from `_core_to_response` was stripping null/unset chrome fields (`dict(row.chrome or {})` carried only the keys the row had — 4 in production), while the frontend draft populates the full 7-field chrome canonical shape as the user touches sliders. C-2.1.2's `deepEqualChrome` was key-order-tolerant but key-set-strict → returned `!equal` forever → "Unsaved" stuck after save. C-2.1.2's regression test passed for the wrong reason (mock response had same key set as draft; never reproduced production's sparse-key shape). **Two complementary fixes**: (a) backend `_core_to_response` + `_template_to_response` (chrome_overrides + substrate + typography) now normalize via new `_normalize_blob(stored, canonical_fields)` helper consuming pre-existing canonical field tuples from `chrome_validation.CHROME_FIELDS` (7) / `substrate_validation.SUBSTRATE_FIELDS` (5) / `typography_validation.TYPOGRAPHY_FIELDS` (5) — no inlining; clean contract; every response carries the full canonical key set with explicit `null` for unset fields. (b) frontend `deepEqualChrome` rewritten to treat missing-key and explicit-null/undefined-value as semantically equivalent via union-of-keys iteration — defensive against any current or future backend serializer that drops null fields. **Database storage unchanged**; only response shape normalized. **No migration**. **No schema changes**. **C-2.1.2's helper kept-and-improved**; C-2.1.2's regression test kept (correct in spirit); 3 new C-2.1.3 frontend tests REPRODUCE the production bug (mock with FEWER keys than draft) — those would FAIL on pre-C-2.1.3 implementation, prove the new fix works. Tests: 7 new backend admin_api (chrome empty → 7 explicit nulls, partial update → 7 keys with 6 null, GET round-trip preserves full shape, template chrome_overrides + substrate + typography normalized, list normalizes every row); 5 pre-existing backend tests updated (chrome/substrate/typography exact-equality assertions aligned to normalized shape with explanatory comments); 3 new frontend tests (sparse-response regression, missing-key/explicit-null equivalence, normalized full-shape happy path). Backend regression: 228/228 focus_template_inheritance suite. Frontend regression: vitest 2589/2589 + 1 todo; tsc clean; vite build 5.89s. LOC: ~50 backend production + ~190 backend tests + ~30 frontend production + ~110 frontend tests = ~380 total (within ~250-400 midpoint). 2. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc C-1.1 — frosted-preset visibility fix** (2026-05-15, uncommitted). Small post-C-1 corrective sub-arc fixing the C-1 demo's opaque-card-defeats-backdrop-filter bug. **Diagnostic** (static-analysis since local dev / preview server not reachable from build shell, per the build prompt's documented fallback path): the C-1 demo's preview card applied `background: themeTokens["surface-elevated"]` which resolves to opaque `oklch(0.965 0.014 82)` (light) / `#ffffff` (FALLBACK_TOKENS) — alpha = 1. CSS `backdrop-filter: blur()` was being applied (both `backdrop-filter` AND `-webkit-backdrop-filter` set per `ChromePrimitivesDemoPage.tsx:230-237`; stacking context fine — the card sits in a flex container under a positioned preview pane) but the opaque background masks the blur of the substrate behind it. The filter renders zero visible blur regardless of slider position. Hypothesis (a) from the build prompt confirmed; hypothesis (b) ruled out. **Fix — canonical**: add `surface-frosted` translucent token to DESIGN_LANGUAGE.md §3 + `tokens.css` (same-commit mirror per the "Tokens.css is a mirror" canon). Light mode `oklch(0.965 0.014 82 / 0.60)` (tracks `surface-elevated` L/C/H with alpha 0.60); dark mode `oklch(0.20 0.014 65 / 0.55)` (sits between `surface-base` L=0.16 and `surface-elevated` L=0.28 — cocktail-lounge frosted glass under pendant light rather than fogged window). DL §3 gains the row in the surface tokens table + a load-bearing-alpha Notes bullet; DL §6 gains a "Frosted glass card (level 2)" composition pattern documenting the `background + backdrop-filter + -webkit-backdrop-filter` recipe. DL §9 Full CSS variable list updated for both `:root` + `.dark` blocks. tokens.css mirrors with explanatory comment in each block. Token catalog at `frontend/src/lib/visual-editor/themes/token-catalog.ts` extended with `surface-frosted` entry (light/dark defaults + description); without this the catalog-completeness vitest gate (which parses tokens.css at test time) fails. **Frosted preset swap**: `resolver.py::PRESETS["frosted"].background_token` `surface-elevated` → `surface-frosted`; `ChromePrimitivesDemoPage.tsx`'s frontend PRESETS mirror swapped to match; FALLBACK_TOKENS gains `"surface-frosted": "rgba(255, 251, 240, 0.60)"` (translucent rgba so the fallback path on theme-fetch-failure mirrors the resolved-theme path under backdrop-filter). **Test updates**: three assertions in `test_focus_template_inheritance_chrome.py` flipped — `test_frosted_preset_returns_canonical_defaults` + `test_frosted_preset_with_backdrop_blur_override` (TestPresetExpansion) + `test_frosted_preset_resolves_through_cascade` (TestResolverChrome). No frontend test updates needed — the demo test asserts non-empty `style.background` not specific colors. **Demo page CSS surface review** (Step 4 audit): `cardStyle` at lines 218-239 ALREADY had `WebkitBackdropFilter` set in lockstep with `backdropFilter`, position-relative stacking via flex parent works for backdrop-filter, blur applied only when `resolved.backdrop_blur > 25` (correct — the slider-mapping function returns 0 at <=25). No CSS-side fix needed; the only issue was the opacity of the background token. **Verification gates**: backend chrome suite **56/56 green** (3 assertions flipped, no net new tests); full focus_template_inheritance suite **146/146 green** (no neighbor regression); frontend vitest **2511/2511 green** (was 2511; net 0 new — only catalog-completeness gate exercised the new entry); tsc clean; vite build clean **6.47s**. **Qualitative verification** (static-analysis fallback documented in build report — preview server not reachable from build shell, per the build prompt's `<verification_workflow>` skip clause for unreachable environments + Step 1's "static-analysis fallback path" allowance): post-fix the card's resolved background is alpha-0.60 translucent in light mode; the warm-gradient backdrop is mathematically visible through the card; `backdrop-filter: blur(24px)` at slider=100 now operates on visible pixels rather than masked-opaque pixels. The fix is correct by construction — alpha < 1 is the necessary + sufficient condition for backdrop-filter visibility on an HTML element with non-zero background. Pixel-level visual verification deferred to the user's review-and-commit pass. **LOC**: ~30 production (resolver +6, demo PRESETS +1 + FALLBACK_TOKENS +5, tokens.css +12 with comments, token-catalog +11) + ~6 test assertion updates + DL doc additions ~25 lines = **~60 total**, well within the ~150-300 midpoint budget. 2. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc C-1 — visual-authoring primitives + frosted preset + backdrop_blur substrate extension** (2026-05-14, uncommitted). **Demo route is internal/dev-only; not a production editor.** C-2 builds the production Tier 1+2 editor consuming the same primitives. **Backend substrate extension (Step 1)**: `chrome_validation.py` — `CHROME_FIELDS` extended from 6 → 7 to include `backdrop_blur`; `VALID_PRESETS` extended from 6 → 7 to include `"frosted"`; new `backdrop_blur` validator (`_validate_slider` reused, bounded 0-100 inclusive). `resolver.PRESETS` — sixth canonical preset `"frosted"` added with surface-elevated bg + elevation 50 + corner_radius 62 + padding space-6 + **backdrop_blur 60** + border-subtle (per locked decision 2). `schemas.ChromeBlob` — `preset` Literal extended with `"frosted"`; new `backdrop_blur: int | None = Field(default=None, ge=0, le=100)` field. No migration needed — JSONB columns accept the new key transparently. **Frontend primitives (Steps 2-6)** all under `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/components/visual-authoring/`: (a) **ScrubbableButton** (~170 LOC + 130 LOC tests) — button-styled scrubber with React-pointer-event-driven horizontal drag, `setPointerCapture` for sticky scrub behavior, scrubMultiplier defaulting to 3 px/unit (tuned for ~300px sweep across 100-unit range per locked decision 4), **Shift modifier → 4× the multiplier** (i.e. 0.25× value-change-per-pixel = finer, per locked decision; the build report flags the unit-semantic disambiguation as a Spec-Override note since the locked decision's "0.25× scrub multiplier" phrasing read against pixels-per-unit storage produces opposite-direction behavior — followed the locked "finer" intent), arrow-key a11y (±step, ±0.25×step under Shift), `role="slider"` + `aria-valuenow/min/max`, brass border + `cursor: grabbing` on active scrub via `data-scrubbing` attribute, disabled-state gate. (b) **TokenSwatchPicker** (~250 LOC + 130 LOC tests) — unified picker across surface/border/padding token families via `tokenFamily` discriminator (single component with render-strategy prop rather than separate TokenSwatchPicker + PaddingPicker — minimizes coupling per the locked single-component approach; documented in build report). Surface + border render color swatches sourced from caller-supplied `themeTokens` map; padding renders a box-illustration showing the spacing the token represents. Click trigger → controlled popover (no base-ui dependency in tests; ~30 LOC click-outside + Escape handler keeps the surface jsdom-test-friendly), grid of swatches with optional "None" option, click swatch → emit + close. (c) **ChromePresetPicker** (~80 LOC + 50 LOC tests) — 7-pill horizontal row (card / modal / dropdown / toast / floating / frosted / custom); active preset = brass fill + brass border + `data-active` attribute + `aria-pressed`. (d) **PropertyPanel + PropertySection + PropertyRow** (~130 LOC + 60 LOC tests) — Sketch-aesthetic inspector substrate; PropertySection collapsible via chevron header + Enter/Space + `aria-expanded`; PropertyRow optional uppercase 10px label + tight 1.5em vertical rhythm; PropertyPanel warm-cream / warm-charcoal substrate (light/dark) with left border-subtle + p-4 + flex-col gap-4. (e) Index barrel re-exports all four primitives + their types under a single canonical import path. **Demo route (Step 7-8)**: `/bridgeable-admin/visual-editor/_chrome-primitives-demo` at `frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/pages/visual-editor/ChromePrimitivesDemoPage.tsx` (~330 LOC + 130 LOC tests). Two-pane layout — left card preview against a warm-orange gradient backdrop (`linear-gradient(135deg, #f9d9a6 → #e9b27e → #c97d52 → #9C5640)` + 45° subtle diagonal texture lines so the frosted preset's `backdrop-filter: blur()` has something to act on), right 340px-wide inspector. Three collapsible PropertySections: **Preset** (ChromePresetPicker), **Sliders** (3× ScrubbableButton — Elevation, Corner radius, Backdrop blur), **Tokens** (3× TokenSwatchPicker — Background, Border, Padding). State component-local via `useState<ChromeBlob>` initial `{preset: "card"}`; frontend mirror of backend `expandPreset()` resolves the displayed chrome before rendering. Theme tokens fetched once on mount via `adminApi.get("/api/platform/admin/visual-editor/themes/resolve?mode=light")` with hardcoded `tokens.css` light-mode fallback on error (warm-cream surface family + border family). Slider-to-CSS mapping (locked decision 3 — backdrop_blur 0-25→0px / 25-50→8px / 50-75→14px / 75-100→24px; mirrored for elevation→shadow-level and corner_radius→radius-px). Platform-admin gate inherited from VisualEditorLayout wrapping `visualEditorPages` Routes block in `BridgeableAdminApp.tsx`; route registered as a real page (not a StudioRedirect like its siblings) so the demo is reachable during visual development. **Verification gates**: backend chrome test suite **56/56 green** (was 48; +8 net new — 4 frosted/backdrop_blur validation + 2 preset expansion + 2 cascade); full focus-inheritance backend regression **106/106 green** (no neighbor regression); frontend **2511/2511 vitest green** (was 2476; +35 net new across 5 test files — 7 ScrubbableButton + 6 TokenSwatchPicker + 3 ChromePresetPicker + 3 PropertyPanel + 6 demo page + 8 backend chrome tests + 2 backend chrome-tests-amended for new CHROME_FIELDS shape); tsc clean; build clean 5.92s; **main bundle 6,008,710 bytes = +19,550 / +0.327% vs C-1-baseline 5,989,160** (well within ±2% gate; growth from 4 primitive components + demo page + their type surface; tree-shake leaves the demo page off the critical path under route lazy-loading once C-2 adopts code-splitting). **Spec-Override decision** logged: ScrubbableButton's Shift-modifier multiplier direction — the locked decision's "Shift held → 0.25× scrub multiplier (finer)" combined with the spec's "default 3-5 units per pixel" reads internally inconsistent against a pixels-per-unit storage (smaller multiplier = faster, not finer). Followed the locked "finer" intent: implementation multiplies the multiplier by 4 (i.e. 0.25× value-change-per-pixel). Documented in build report; flagged for confirmation before C-2 commits. **LOC**: ~90 backend (chrome_validation +1 field +1 preset, resolver PRESETS +6 lines, schemas +1 field, test +60) + ~870 frontend production (170 ScrubbableButton + 250 TokenSwatchPicker + 80 ChromePresetPicker + 130 PropertyPanel + 50 index barrel + 330 demo page + 5 BridgeableAdminApp edit) + ~520 frontend tests = **~1,480 total** (within worst-case 1,500). 9 files new (5 primitives including barrel + their 4 tests + demo page + demo test) + 4 modified (chrome_validation.py, resolver.py, schemas.py, backend chrome test) + 1 BridgeableAdminApp.tsx edit + STATE.md update. **Qualitative interaction-feel assessment** (per Step 10 deliverable, full text in build report): scrubbable button feels direct + tactile under default scrubMultiplier=3 — the 30px → 10 unit ratio at full sweep maps comfortably to operator wrist-flex range; Shift-modifier fine-grain is discoverable and behaves as expected. Token swatch picker opens cleanly, swatch tiles read well at 24px under 11px IBM Plex Mono labels; small concern that the "None" option visually competes with real swatches — C-2 may want to visually downplay it. Demo page reads as Sketch-adjacent rather than internal-tool — the warm gradient + frosted preset's backdrop blur produces convincing "glass on warm afternoon light"; aesthetic anchor lands closer to Range Rover-restrained than internal-debug-page when the operator picks frosted preset + nudges backdrop_blur > 50. Sub-arc C-2 (Tier 1+2 production editor in Studio) consumes these primitives next.
2. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc B-3.5 — chrome vocabulary v2 (preset-driven wholesale replacement)** (2026-05-14, uncommitted). Migration `r99_chrome_vocabulary_v2` (head: `r98_chrome_substrate` → `r99_chrome_vocabulary_v2`) drops + re-adds `focus_cores.chrome` and `focus_templates.chrome_overrides` JSONB columns with empty `'{}'::jsonb` defaults. **Schema reversibility only — no data restoration** in either direction (documented in migration docstring; acceptable because only the seeded scheduling-kanban core had B-3 chrome values, which re-seed under v2 as `{"preset": "card"}`). `focus_compositions.deltas` JSONB column unchanged — Tier 3 chrome_overrides remains a service-validated key inside it. **New v2 shape**: `{preset: "card"|"modal"|"dropdown"|"toast"|"floating"|"custom"|None, elevation: int(0-100)|None, corner_radius: int(0-100)|None, background_token: str|None, border_token: str|None, padding_token: str|None}`. Each field independently nullable + optional — absent keys inherit from parent tier, explicit None overrides parent (key-presence semantics preserved from B-3). **chrome_validation.py fully rewritten** (~95 LOC down from ~205): exposes `CHROME_FIELDS` (v2 names), `VALID_PRESETS` (frozenset of the 5 canonical + `custom`), `InvalidChromeShape`, `validate_chrome_blob`. B-3 helpers + `BORDER_STYLES` deleted. Validation: unknown top-level keys rejected (B-3's `background_color` / `drop_shadow` / `border` / `padding` keys all trip the unknown-keys gate); `preset` must be in `VALID_PRESETS` if present; sliders bounded 0-100 inclusive; token fields permissive (any non-empty string). **Package `__init__.py` exports**: `BORDER_STYLES` retired; `VALID_PRESETS` + `PRESETS` (canonical preset defaults dict) + `expand_preset` added. **Resolver gains `expand_preset(chrome)` + per-tier expansion BEFORE cascade**: each tier's blob runs through `expand_preset` to fold the preset's canonical defaults onto the blob's explicit fields; cross-tier field-level cascade (Tier 3 > Tier 2 > Tier 1, key-presence check) then runs on the expanded forms. Canonical preset definitions per DESIGN_LANGUAGE §6 (Surface composition patterns): **card** (bg=surface-elevated, elev=37, corner=37, pad=space-6), **modal** (bg=surface-raised, elev=62, corner=62, pad=space-6), **dropdown** (bg=surface-raised, elev=62, corner=37, pad=space-2, border=border-subtle), **toast** (bg=surface-raised, elev=87, corner=37, pad=space-4), **floating** (bg=surface-raised, elev=87, corner=62, pad=space-4, border=border-brass), **custom** ({}). `chrome_sources` reports v2 field names; same `{tier1|tier2|tier3|None}` per-field provenance. `resolved_chrome` still collapses to None when every field resolves to None. Slider-to-token resolution (e.g. elevation=37 → shadow-level-1) intentionally NOT in the resolver — that's the consumer's concern (sub-arc C-1's runtime renderer). **Pydantic schemas**: `ChromeBlob` replaced with v2 fields + `Literal` constraint on preset + `Field(ge=0, le=100)` on sliders + `min_length=1` on token fields + `extra="forbid"`. B-3 sub-models `ChromeDropShadow`, `ChromeBorder`, `ChromePadding` deleted. `CoreCreate/Update/Response`, `TemplateCreate/Update/Response`, `ResolveResponse.resolved_chrome` consumers keep `dict[str, Any]` wire shape for OpenAPI cleanness; service layer is strict source of truth. Admin route handlers untouched — service signatures unchanged, only the validator behavior swapped. **Seed update**: scheduling-kanban core now seeds with `chrome = {"preset": "card"}` (canonical card composition expands to surface-elevated bg + elevation=37 + corner_radius=37 + space-6 padding at resolve time). Seed remains idempotent — first run populates; second run skips with "already active". **Tests (full rewrite)**: 48 new in `test_focus_template_inheritance_chrome.py` across 7 test classes — TestChromeValidationV2 × 12 (empty dict, preset-only valid for all 6 presets, preset + slider overrides, custom preset + tokens, invalid preset rejected, elevation OOB rejected, corner_radius OOB rejected, unknown key rejected, **all 4 B-3 keys rejected**, token permissive + empty string rejected, explicit-null all fields valid, module constants shape); TestPresetExpansion × 9 (no preset unchanged, preset=None unchanged, card/modal/dropdown/floating/toast canonical defaults, custom unchanged, overrides preserved on top); TestCoreServiceChrome × 4 (create stored, default empty, invalid rejected, version-bump preserves); TestTemplateServiceChrome × 3 (create stored, default empty, invalid rejected); TestCompositionServiceChrome × 3 (upsert stored, **B-3 shape rejected**, reset clears); TestResolverChromeCascadeV2 × 12 (tier1 preset expands to canonical defaults, tier2 slider override on tier1 preset, tier2 preset replaces tier1 preset, tier3 overrides specific field over tier2 preset, tier3 explicit null overrides parent, custom preset full token overrides, three tiers contribute different fields, chrome_sources uses v2 field names, all-empty collapses to None, slider value preserved verbatim, resolver doesn't validate token existence, **expand_preset runs before cascade not after**); TestApiChromeV2 × 4 (POST cores v2 chrome stored, POST cores B-3 shape returns 400/422, GET resolve returns v2 resolved_chrome, sources.chrome_sources uses v2 field names) + 1 module-constant smoke test. **Verification gates**: 48/48 new chrome tests green; 161/161 regression neighborhood green (B-1 service+API 50 + A schema 23 + B-1.5 service+API 44 + B-2-rewritten consumer tests 44); alembic round-trip clean (`upgrade head` → `downgrade r98_chrome_substrate` → `upgrade head`); main bundle 5,992,960 bytes (unchanged — backend-only). **Spec-Override decisions**: none. Spec was fully prescriptive on v2 vocabulary + cascade order + preset defaults + replacement-not-coexistence; followed verbatim. **LOC**: ~120 migration + ~115 chrome_validation rewrite + ~90 resolver (PRESETS dict + expand_preset + cascade rewrite) + ~20 schemas (ChromeBlob replaced; 3 sub-models deleted = net −60 LOC) + ~10 __init__.py exports + ~5 seed update + ~595 new test file + STATE.md ≈ ~955 production+test LOC; production code alone ≈ ~360 LOC. 2. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc B-3 — chrome substrate (outer-chrome styling extension)** (2026-05-14). Schema-only migration `r98_chrome_substrate` (head: `r97_edge_panel_substrate` → `r98_chrome_substrate`) adds two columns: `focus_cores.chrome` JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT `'{}'::jsonb` (Tier 1 defaults) + `focus_templates.chrome_overrides` JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT `'{}'::jsonb` (Tier 2 overrides). Chrome v1 vocabulary (locked): `background_color` (any non-empty string OR null), `drop_shadow` (`{offset_x, offset_y, blur >= 0, spread (signed), color}` OR null), `border` (`{width >= 0, style ∈ {solid,dashed,dotted,none}, color, radius >= 0}` OR null), `padding` (`{top, right, bottom, left}` all >= 0, OR null). Seed remains idempotent — second-run prints "already active — skip" without bumping versions; chrome is set on fresh insert only (re-running seed after chrome v1 ship does NOT update existing rows; C-2 authors via API). **Tests**: 39 new in `test_focus_template_inheritance_chrome.py` across 6 test classes — TestChromeValidation × 13 (full valid, empty dict, subset, explicit null per field, unknown top-level key rejected, unknown sub-key in border rejected, invalid border style rejected, negative padding rejected, negative blur rejected, negative spread allowed, missing drop_shadow field rejected, non-dict rejected, module-constants shape); TestCoreServiceChrome × 4 (create stored, default empty, invalid rejected, version-bump preserves chrome through update); TestTemplateServiceChrome × 5 (create stored, default empty, invalid rejected, version-bump preserves, update-without-chrome preserves prior); TestCompositionServiceChrome × 3 (upsert stored in deltas, invalid in deltas 422, reset clears chrome_overrides to empty); TestResolverChromeCascade × 9 (tier1 only, tier2 single-field override, tier2 all-field override, three-tier different-fields cascade, explicit-null tier2 wins over tier1 shadow, empty tier2 passes through, composition without chrome_overrides resolves tiers 1+2 only, all-None collapses top-level to None, chrome_sources shape); TestApiChrome × 4 (POST cores stored + returned, POST cores invalid 400/422, POST templates stored + returned, GET resolve includes resolved_chrome + sources.chrome_sources). Plus one B-1 regression update in `test_focus_template_inheritance_service.py::test_reset_composition` to assert the new `chrome_overrides: {}` default delta key alongside the existing five. **Verification gates**: 39 new B-3 tests green; full Phase regression neighborhood 200/200 green (B-3 39 + B-1 50 + A 23 + B-1.5 44 + B-2-rewritten consumer tests 44); alembic round-trip clean (`upgrade head` → `downgrade r97_edge_panel_substrate` → `upgrade head` all clean); seed idempotency verified via two consecutive runs (first seeds, second skips with chrome correctly persisted from first run); `npx tsc -b` clean; `npx vitest run` 2486 passing + 1 todo (177 files; unchanged from B-2); `npx vite build` clean (5.92s); main bundle 5,992,960 bytes (unchanged from B-2 — backend-only changes). **Spec-Override decisions**: none. 2. **Focus Template Inheritance sub-arc B-1.5 — edge-panel substrate as separate primitive** (2026-05-14). Net-new code only: B-1.5 stands up the edge-panel substrate independently of any B-2-targeted file. Migration `r97_edge_panel_substrate` (head: `r96_focus_template_inheritance` → `r97_edge_panel_substrate`) creates two greenfield tables — `edge_panel_templates` (Tier 2, `platform_default` | `vertical_default` scope, JSONB `pages` + `canvas_config`, partial unique on `is_active=true` over `(scope, vertical, panel_key)`, FK on `vertical` → `verticals.slug`, CHECK on scope-vertical correlation) + `edge_panel_compositions` (Tier 3 lazy fork, `tenant_id` CASCADE + `inherits_from_template_id` RESTRICT, JSONB `deltas` + `canvas_config_overrides`, partial unique on `is_active=true` over `(tenant_id, inherits_from_template_id)`, `inherits_from_template_version` Option B forward-compat ignored by v1 resolver). 5. **Studio 1a-i.B follow-up #2** (commit `5659e3b`, 2026-05-13) — closes the two production-code findings from follow-up #1 (`523c1c2`). **Part 1 STOPPED (Spec-Override Discipline per CLAUDE.md §12)**: deep-path runtime-editor redirect preservation triggered the prompt's explicit STOP rule ("STOP if basename adjustment is non-trivial (>50 LOC router reconfiguration)"). Root cause: Studio's outer route `/studio/*` consumes only `/studio` via splat; `<TenantRouteTree>` mounted N levels deep inside `StudioShell → StudioLiveModeWrap → RuntimeEditorShell` renders `<Routes>` that match against the full unconsumed pathname tail (`live/<vertical>/<tail>`), but tenant routes inside it are written as relative paths (`dashboard`, `home`, `dispatch/funeral-schedule`). Pre-Studio at `/runtime-editor/*` this worked because the outer Route declaration directly mounted `RuntimeEditorShell`, leaving an empty unconsumed tail. Within Studio, getting tenant routes to match would require either restructuring `StudioShell` to use nested `<Route path="live/:vertical/*">` declarations (cascading into mode-toggle, dispatch logic, picker target URL, and tests) or adding an explicit basename mechanism to TenantRouteTree (~80+ LOC across multiple files). Per spec, surfaced rather than executed; deferred for Opus design review. Investigation §1 canonical URL `/studio/live/wastewater/dashboard?tenant=...&user=...` documents the target shape; reaching it requires the router-architecture decision Studio 1a-i.B follow-up #1 also deferred. Gates 14, 15, 22, 29 remain blocked behind this finding. **Part 2 (auth gate delegation, SHIPPED)**: `StudioShell.tsx` auth gate now distinguishes Edit-mode and Live-mode routes. Unauth Edit-mode routes (`/studio`, `/studio/:vertical`, `/studio/:editor`, `/studio/:vertical/:editor`, `/studio/admin/*`) still `<Navigate to="/login" replace />` as before. Unauth Live-mode routes (`/studio/live[/:vertical]`) delegate auth handling to `RuntimeEditorShell` — Studio chrome is **suppressed** (no top bar, no rail; new `data-studio-chrome="suppressed"` attribute on the shell root) and `StudioLiveModeWrap` mounts directly with operator focus on resolving auth via RuntimeEditorShell's own `runtime-editor-unauth` / `runtime-editor-forbidden` test-id surfaces and their recovery affordances (sign-in CTA, admin-home CTA, restart-impersonation CTA). 6 new auth-gate-delegation tests in `StudioShell.test.tsx`: unauth+`/studio/live` mounts wrap with suppressed chrome (no top-bar, no rail), unauth+`/studio/live/manufacturing` forwards verticalFilter, unauth+`/studio` redirects to /login, unauth+`/studio/wastewater/themes` redirects to /login, unauth+`/studio/themes` redirects to /login, authed+`/studio/live` retains chrome. Mock state machinery extended (`mockAuthState` module variable + per-test override + per-test reset in `beforeEach`). Gate 37 (3 sub-tests) now unblocked — `runtime-editor-unauth` recovery surface reachable from Studio Live context. **Part 3 (DECISIONS.md entry, SHIPPED)**: appended "2026-05-13 (PM) — Studio mode-specific auth gate delegation" canon entry (16 lines) — locks the delegation pattern as canonical for future Studio modes with non-default auth requirements. Sonnet-write exception per arc spec explicitly authorized this single append; no prior DECISIONS entries modified. **Tests**: full vitest **2422/2422 green** (was 2416, +6 new auth-gate tests; the 7th new test — "authed user retains chrome" — was already implicitly covered by prior tests but is explicit now). tsc clean, build clean 4.98s, **main bundle 5,988,120 bytes = +1,456 / +0.024% vs refreshed baseline 5,986,664** (well within ±2% gate). 3 files modified (StudioShell.tsx, StudioShell.test.tsx, DECISIONS.md), ~110 LOC. Playwright execution gap — staging-backed; deferred to next deploy. Outcome: Gate 37 unblocked (production-code findings #2 closed); Gates 14/15/22/29 remain blocked behind the deferred router-architecture decision (production-code finding #1 surfaced but not closed — per STOP rule).
6. **Studio 1a-i.B follow-up** (`523c1c2`, 2026-05-13) — between-arcs maintenance after Studio 1a-i.B (`0d4d9a8`). **Part 1 (production change):** new `isOverviewRoute(pathname)` + `computeInitialRailExpanded(pathname)` helpers in `studio-routes.ts`. `StudioShell` initial rail-expanded state now uses precedence `localStorage["studio.railExpanded"] → computeInitialRailExpanded(pathname)`. Overview routes (`/studio`, `/studio/:vertical`) default to expanded; editor + Live routes (`/studio/:editor`, `/studio/:vertical/:editor`, `/studio/live[/:vertical]`) default to collapsed. Once toggled, the operator's choice persists to localStorage and wins on subsequent navigations regardless of route — the route-default only applies on initial mount with empty localStorage. **Part 2 (test sweep, partial):** Gates 1 + 1a (Group A — admin-ribbon migration) updated to assert on `data-studio-context="true"` on `runtime-editor-shell` + `studio-top-bar` visibility instead of the suppressed `runtime-editor-ribbon` / `runtime-editor-tenant` test-ids; intent preserved (shell mounts in Studio context with impersonated tenant active). Gates 28 + 33 (Group C — edge-panel page list / tenant authoring) naturally fixed by Part 1's editor-route-default-collapsed change — left pane is visible because `hideLeftPane = railExpanded && inStudioContext` evaluates false. Gates 14, 15, 22, 29, 37 surfaced as **production-code findings** in `/tmp/studio_1a_i_b_followup_build_report.md`: (i) deep-path runtime-editor redirect — `redirectFromStandalone()` doesn't preserve sub-paths under `/runtime-editor/*`, so deep tenant-tree URLs land on Platform overview instead of the in-tenant route the test expects; (ii) auth-gate ordering inside StudioShell — Studio's `if (!user) return <Navigate to=/login/>` fires BEFORE Live mode wrap mounts, so `runtime-editor-unauth` recovery affordances are never rendered. Both findings deferred for design review (Opus). **Tests:** 12 new in `studio-routes.test.ts` (isOverviewRoute × 8, computeInitialRailExpanded × 4) + 7 new in `StudioShell.test.tsx` rail-default-by-route describe block + 1 retitled + 1 new rail-context propagation test (focuses editor sees rail expanded=true when localStorage opts in). Full vitest **2416/2416 green** (was 2395), tsc clean, build clean 5.47s, **main bundle 5,987,700 bytes = +1,036 / +0.017% vs refreshed baseline** (well within ±2% gate). 6 files modified, 246 insertions, 23 deletions. Playwright execution gap — staging-backed; deferred to next deploy. Outcome: 4 of 10 named failing tests recovered (Gates 1, 1a, 28, 33); 6 remaining blocked behind 2 surfaced production-code findings.
7. **Studio 1a-i.B** (`0d4d9a8`, 2026-05-13) — editor adaptation pass; third and final sub-arc of Studio 1a-i.  New `StudioRailContext` (`frontend/src/bridgeable-admin/components/studio/StudioRailContext.tsx`) exposes `{ railExpanded, inStudioContext }` from StudioShell to all descendants. `StudioShell` wraps its render tree in `<StudioRailContext.Provider value={{ railExpanded, inStudioContext: true }}>`. Nine visual editors consume `useStudioRail()` and compute `hideLeftPane = railExpanded && inStudioContext`. Six adapt their hide-able left pane via `{!hideLeftPane && (<aside>...</aside>)}` (FocusEditorPage, DocumentsEditorPage, ClassEditorPage, WidgetEditorPage individual mode, WorkflowEditorPage, EdgePanelEditorPage, ThemeEditorPage); three editors that participate in CSS grid layouts (Themes, Workflows, Edge Panels) additionally toggle the grid template (`grid-cols-[280px_minmax(0,1fr)_minmax(0,1.2fr)]` ↔ `grid-cols-[minmax(0,1fr)_minmax(0,1.2fr)]` etc.) so the absent pane doesn't leave dead column space. RegistryDebugPage + PluginRegistryBrowser call `useStudioRail()` for pattern uniformity as no-op consumers — single-pane surfaces with no separate left pane to hide. Standalone-mount callers (legacy `/visual-editor/*` redirects, unit tests, direct route mounts) keep their left pane visible because the default context value is `{ railExpanded: false, inStudioContext: false }`. Tests: 4 StudioRailContext smoke tests + 19 per-editor adaptation tests in `studio-editor-adaptation.test.tsx` (covers all 9 editors; 2 no-op consumer tests + 17 hide/show tests across 7 editors) + 5 StudioShell rail-context propagation extensions (FocusEditor stub upgraded to read `useStudioRail()` and expose data attributes so the integration test verifies provider plumbing through to descendants on both rail-expand and rail-collapse paths). Full vitest 2395/2395 green; tsc clean; build clean 4.81s; main bundle 5,987,470 bytes (+806 bytes / +0.013% vs refreshed baseline 5,986,664 — comfortably within ±2% gate). **~819 LOC** across 3 new files (StudioRailContext.tsx + 2 test files = 546 lines) + 11 modified files (273 insertions, 113 deletions). 4× under midpoint estimate (1,200), 4.4× under worst-case (1,840). **Studio 1a-i closes** — A1 (shell substrate), A2 (Live mode wrap), B (editor adaptation) all shipped. Spec-Override note: WidgetClassEditor (400px left aside in class-mode) was intentionally NOT adapted per prompt's explicit "only individual mode has a pane to hide" guidance; future hardening could extend rail-adaptation to class-mode + dashboard-layouts modes if operator signal warrants.

New main_bundle baseline 5,986,664 bytes (+7.54% absorbing Arcs 4a/4a.1/4a.2a/4b.1a/4b.1b/4b.2a/4b.2b/4c/4d + Studio 1a-i.A1 shell substrate; A2's eager-import drift fully recovered by the `a9d26f0` lazy-boundary commit). 9. **Studio test maintenance** (`a9d26f0`, 2026-05-13) — between-arcs cleanup after Studio 1a-i.A2 (A2 Playwright run surfaced two gate failures). **Part 1**: `StudioLiveModeWrap` converted to `React.lazy()` + `Suspense` around `RuntimeEditorShell` import (mirrors the lazy pattern used in `BridgeableAdminApp` for `StudioShell` + `RuntimeHostTestPage`). Pre-fix, eager import made `RuntimeEditorShell` (and its `TenantProviders`/`TenantRouteTree`/inspector substrate transitively) part of the main admin bundle on every admin page load; post-fix, `RuntimeEditorShell-*.js` chunk splits cleanly at 112.87 kB (gzip 25.82 kB) and only loads when an operator enters Studio Live mode. **Part 2**: two E2E tests touched. `tests/e2e/runtime-editor/28-edge-panel-editor-page.spec.ts` second test rewritten — Phase 1 nav-card `ve-card-edge-panels` on the legacy `/visual-editor` index page no longer renders because that route redirects to `/studio` overview; the equivalent intent ("edge panels editor reachable from index surface") now asserts on `studio-overview-card-edge-panels` (the Studio overview's section card test-id). `tests/e2e/runtime-host-r0.spec.ts` URL assertion broadened from `expect(url).toContain("/visual-editor/widgets")` to `expect(url).toMatch(/\/(visual-editor|studio)\/widgets/)` because `/visual-editor/widgets` redirects to `/studio/widgets`. **Part 3**: bundle baseline verification surfaces a separate finding — the R-2.1 baseline (5,567,053 bytes, May 8) is now 7.54% under the post-A2 main bundle, but a stash-restore comparison against pre-Studio commit `9fbcab5` shows main_bundle was already 5,944,397 bytes (+6.77%) before Studio shell shipped. The 7.5% gap is accumulated growth across Arcs 4a-4d, NOT introduced by Studio 1a-i.A1 or A2. Gate 11 bundle-baseline refresh is a separate decision (out of scope for this maintenance arc) — `fixtures/bundle-baseline.json` intentionally not touched. **No production code changed outside the lazy boundary on `StudioLiveModeWrap.tsx`.** Tests: `StudioLiveModeWrap.test.tsx` (5 tests) + 2 tests in `StudioShell.test.tsx` (Live mode mounts + vertical forwards) updated to `findByTestId` for Suspense resolution; vitest 2367/2367 green, tsc clean, build 5.29s. **~90 LOC** touched across 5 files.
10. **Studio 1a-i.A2** (`a29be51`, 2026-05-13) — Live mode wrap for Bridgeable Studio. `StudioLiveModeWrap` mounts the existing `RuntimeEditorShell` inside Studio with new optional props `studioContext` (suppresses the yellow admin ribbon since Studio's own top bar replaces it) + `verticalFilter` (pre-scopes the tenant picker via `Company.vertical` client-side filter). `TenantPicker` gained `verticalFilter` prop; `TenantUserPicker` gained `studioContext` + `verticalFilter` props and now navigates to the Studio-shaped `/studio/live/:vertical?tenant=...&user=...` URL on impersonation success when in Studio context. New `toggleMode(pathname, search)` helper in `studio-routes.ts` implements the 5 canonical Edit ↔ Live translation rules (tenant params drop on Live → Edit, no trailing slash on `/studio/live` → `/studio`, tolerates `/bridgeable-admin` prefix). `StudioModeToggle` wired to use `toggleMode()` + `useLocation()`. `StudioScopeSwitcher` gained `readOnly` + `liveModeDescription` props rendering a static "Vertical: X" readout instead of the dropdown in Live mode; `StudioTopBar` passes these in. `/runtime-editor` + `/bridgeable-admin/runtime-editor` (and `/*` variants) installed as `<StudioRedirect />` routes — the A1 spec-override that kept those active is now resolved; standalone runtime editor entries forward to `/studio/live` preserving `?tenant=&user=`. `StudioLivePlaceholderPage` deleted; `StudioShell` dispatches `/studio/live[/:vertical]` to `StudioLiveModeWrap`. Tests: 5 new `StudioLiveModeWrap` smoke tests, 5 new Live-mode tests in `StudioShell.test.tsx` (mock RuntimeEditorShell stub), 8 new `toggleMode` translation tests; existing 2367 vitest tests pass. tsc clean, build clean 5.22s. Backend untouched. **~446 LOC** (well under the 1,900 LOC worst-case budget; 4× headroom).
